// src/components/atoms/Button/Button.jsx
import React from 'react';
import { designTokens } from '../../../design-tokens';

const Button = ({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  disabled = false,
  fullWidth = false,
  onClick,
  type = 'button',
  ...props
}) => {
  // Estilos baseados nos tokens
  const baseStyles = {
    fontFamily: designTokens.typography.fonts.primary,
    fontWeight: designTokens.typography.weights.medium,
    border: 'none',
    borderRadius: designTokens.borders.radius.base,
    cursor: disabled ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
    transition: `all ${designTokens.transitions.duration.fast} ${designTokens.transitions.easing.ease}`,
    display: 'inline-flex',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    gap: designTokens.spacing[2],
    width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
    position: 'relative',
    overflow: 'hidden',
  };

  // Variantes
  const variants = {
    primary: {
      backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[500],
      color: '#FFFFFF',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[600],
        boxShadow: designTokens.shadows.hover,
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: 'none',
        boxShadow: designTokens.shadows.focus,
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[700],
        transform: 'translateY(1px)',
      },
    },
    secondary: {
      backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.secondary[500],
      color: '#FFFFFF',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.secondary[600],
        boxShadow: designTokens.shadows.hover,
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: designTokens.colors.neutral[700],
      border: `2px solid ${designTokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
       

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## 1. ADR-001: Stack Principal V12

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

### CONTEXTO:
A V11 utilizava React 16, Node.js 14 e MongoDB. Necessitamos de uma stack mais moderna com melhor performance, tipagem forte e suporte a longo prazo. O sistema precisa ser 100% autônomo com alta disponibilidade.

### DECISÃO:
Adotar a seguinte stack principal:
- **Frontend:** React 18 com TypeScript 5, Vite como build tool
- **Backend:** Node.js 20 LTS com TypeScript, Express.js com estrutura modular
- **Banco de Dados:** PostgreSQL 16 (principal) + Redis 7 (cache/sessões)
- **Filas:** BullMQ com Redis como backend
- **Monitoramento:** OpenTelemetry com Jaeger e Prometheus
- **Containerização:** Docker + Docker Compose para desenvolvimento

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A:** Manter stack atual (React 16 + Node 14 + MongoDB)
  - Prós: Zero migração, time já conhece
  - Contras: Versões desatualizadas, suporte limitado, performance inferior
- **Opção B:** Next.js 14 + Node.js 20
  - Prós: SSR nativo, otimizações automáticas
  - Contras: Menor flexibilidade, vendor lock-in parcial
- **Opção C:** React 18 + Node.js 20 (escolhida)
  - Prós: Moderno, LTS longo, flexibilidade total, TypeScript nativo
  - Contras: Necessidade de configuração manual

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Melhor performance com React 18 (concorrência, streaming SSR)
- Node.js 20 com melhor segurança e performance
- PostgreSQL com ACID garantido e JSONB para flexibilidade
- TypeScript em todo o stack para maior confiabilidade

**Negativas:**
- Curva de aprendizado para desenvolvedores não familiarizados
- Necessidade de migração de dados do MongoDB
- Configuração inicial mais complexa

**Riscos:**
- Migração de dados pode causar downtime
- Mitigação: Migração em fases com dual-write temporário

## 2. Engineering Standards V12

```markdown
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V12

## Estrutura de Projeto
```
project/
├── frontend/
│   ├── src/
│   │   ├── components/     # Componentes React reutilizáveis
│   │   ├── hooks/         # Custom hooks
│   │   ├── services/      # API clients
│   │   ├── types/         # TypeScript definitions
│   │   └── utils/         # Utilities
│   ├── public/
│   └── package.json
├── backend/
│   ├── src/
│   │   ├── api/          # Rotas Express
│   │   ├── controllers/  # Lógica de negócio
│   │   ├── models/       # Modelos de dados
│   │   ├── services/     # Serviços de domínio
│   │   ├── middleware/   # Middlewares
│   │   ├── utils/        # Utilities
│   │   └── types/        # TypeScript definitions
│   └── package.json
├── shared/               # Código compartilhado
├── docker-compose.yml
└── README.md
```

## Convenções de Código

### TypeScript
- Sempre usar interfaces para objetos
- Evitar `any` - usar `unknown` quando necessário
- Configuração strict ativada

### React
- Functional components com hooks
- Custom hooks para lógica reutilizável
- Componentes pequenos e focados (< 200 linhas)

### Node.js
- Async/await em vez de callbacks
- Error handling centralizado
- Logging estruturado com Winston

## Commits
- Usar Conventional Commits
- Exemplo: `feat: add user authentication`
- Tipos: feat, fix, docs, style, refactor, test, chore

## Testes
- Jest para unit tests
- React Testing Library para componentes
- Supertest para API tests
- Cobertura mínima: 80%
```

## 3. Estratégia de Cache com Redis

```typescript
// backend/src/services/cache.service.ts
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { logger } from '../utils/logger';

export class CacheService {
  private client: Redis;
  private static instance: CacheService;
  private defaultTTL = 3600; // 1 hora

  private constructor() {
    this.client = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
      retryStrategy: (times) => {
        const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
        return delay;
      },
    });

    this.client.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Redis connection error:', err);
    });

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
    });
  }

  static getInstance(): CacheService {
    if (!CacheService.instance) {
      CacheService.instance = new CacheService();
    }
    return CacheService.instance;
  }

  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      const data = await this.client.get(key);
      return data ? JSON.parse(data) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache get error for key ${key}:`, error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async set(key: string, value: any, ttl?: number): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const stringValue = JSON.stringify(value);
      await this.client.setex(key, ttl || this.defaultTTL, stringValue);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache set error for key ${key}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async del(key: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await this.client.del(key);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache delete error for key ${key}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async invalidatePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const keys = await this.client.keys(pattern);
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        await this.client.del(...keys);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache invalidate pattern error for ${pattern}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async healthCheck(): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      await this.client.ping();
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

// Decorator para cache automático
export function Cacheable(ttl?: number, keyPrefix?: string) {
  return function (
    target: any,
    propertyName: string,
    descriptor: PropertyDescriptor
  ) {
    const originalMethod = descriptor.value;
    
    descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
      const cacheService = CacheService.getInstance();
      const cacheKey = keyPrefix 
        ? `${keyPrefix}:${JSON.stringify(args)}`
        : `${propertyName}:${JSON.stringify(args)}`;
      
      // Tentar obter do cache
      const cached = await cacheService.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached !== null) {
        return cached;
      }
      
      // Executar método original
      const result = await originalMethod.apply(this, args);
      
      // Armazenar no cache
      await cacheService.set(cacheKey, result, ttl);
      
      return result;
    };
    
    return descriptor;
  };
}
```

## 4. Sistema de Filas com BullMQ

```typescript
// backend/src/services/queue.service.ts
import { Queue, Worker, QueueEvents } from 'bullmq';
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { logger } from '../utils/logger';

export interface JobData {
  id: string;
  type: string;
  payload: any;
  priority?: number;
}

export class QueueService {
  private connection: Redis;
  private queues: Map<string, Queue> = new Map();
  private workers: Map<string, Worker> = new Map();
  private queueEvents: Map<string, QueueEvents> = new Map();

  constructor() {
    this.connection = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
      maxRetriesPerRequest: null,
    });
  }

  async createQueue(name: string): Promise<Queue> {
    if (this.queues.has(name)) {
      return this.queues.get(name)!;
    }

    const queue = new Queue(name, {
      connection: this.connection,
      defaultJobOptions: {
        attempts: 3,
        backoff: {
          type: 'exponential',
          delay: 1000,
        },
        removeOnComplete: 100,
        removeOnFail: 1000,
      },
    });

    // Configurar eventos da fila
    const queueEvents = new QueueEvents(name, { connection: this.connection });
    
    queueEvents.on('completed', ({ jobId }) => {
      logger.info(`Job ${jobId} completed in queue ${name}`);
    });

    queueEvents.on('failed', ({ jobId, failedReason }) => {
      logger.error(`Job ${jobId} failed in queue ${name}:`, failedReason);
    });

    this.queues.set(name, queue);
    this.queueEvents.set(name, queueEvents);

    return queue;
  }

  async addJob(queueName: string, jobData: JobData): Promise<void> {
    const queue = await this.createQueue(queueName);
    
    await queue.add(
      jobData.type,
      jobData.payload,
      {
        jobId: jobData.id,
        priority: jobData.priority || 1,
      }
    );
  }

  registerWorker<T = any>(
    queueName: string,
    processor: (job: any) => Promise<T>
  ): void {
    if (this.workers.has(queueName)) {
      logger.warn(`Worker for queue ${queueName} already registered`);
      return;
    }

    const worker = new Worker(
      queueName,
      async (job) => {
        logger.info(`Processing job ${job.id} in queue ${queueName}`);
        return await processor(job);
      },
      {
        connection: this.connection,
        concurrency: 5,
        limiter: {
          max: 10,
          duration: 1000,
        },
      }
    );

    worker.on('completed', (job) => {
      logger.info(`Job ${job.id} completed successfully`);
    });

    worker.on('failed', (job, err) => {
      logger.error(`Job ${job?.id} failed:`, err);
    });

    this.workers.set(queueName, worker);
  }

  async getQueueMetrics(queueName: string): Promise<any> {
    const queue = this.queues.get(queueName);
    if (!queue) {
      throw new Error(`Queue ${queueName} not found`);
    }

    const [waiting, active, completed, failed, delayed] = await Promise.all([
      queue.getWaiting(),
      queue.getActive(),
      queue.getCompleted(),
      queue.getFailed(),
      queue.getDelayed(),
    ]);

    return {
      waiting: waiting.length,
      active: active.length,
      completed: completed.length,
      failed: failed.length,
      delayed: delayed.length,
    };
  }

  async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    // Fechar workers
    for (const [name, worker] of this.workers) {
      await worker.close();
      logger.info(`Worker ${name} closed`);
    }

    // Fechar queues
    for (const [name, queue] of this.queues) {
      await queue.close();
      logger.info(`Queue ${name} closed`);
    }

    // Fechar eventos
    for (const [name, events] of this.queueEvents) {
      await events.close();
      logger.info(`Queue events ${name} closed`);
    }

    await this.connection.quit();
  }
}

// Exemplo de uso para processamento assíncrono
export class NotificationService {
  private queueService: QueueService;

  constructor() {
    this.queueService = new QueueService();
    this.setupWorkers();
  }

  private setupWorkers(): void {
    // Worker para emails
    this.queueService.registerWorker('emails', async (job) => {
      const { to, subject, template, data } = job.data;
      // Lógica de envio de email
      return { success: true, messageId: `email-${Date.now()}` };
    });

    // Worker para webhooks
    this.queueService.registerWorker('webhooks', async (job) => {
      const { url, payload } = job.data;
      // Lógica de webhook
      return { success: true, status: 200 };
    });
  }

  async sendEmail(to: string, subject: string, template: string, data: any): Promise<void> {
    await this.queueService.addJob('emails', {
      id: `email-${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`,
      type: 'send-email',
      payload: { to, subject, template, data },
      priority: 2,
    });
  }
}
```

## 5. Monitoramento com OpenTelemetry

```typescript
// backend/src/instrumentation.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { ConsoleSpanExporter } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http';
import { OTLPMetricExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-http';
import { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';
import { ExpressInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-express';
import { HttpInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http';
import { logger } from './utils/logger';

export function initializeTelemetry(serviceName: string): NodeSDK {
  const resource = new Resource({
    [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: serviceName,
    [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: '1.0.0',
    [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  });

  const traceExporter = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production'
    ? new OTLPTraceExporter({
        url: process.env.OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://jaeger:4318/v1/traces',
      })
    : new ConsoleSpanExporter();

  const metricReader = new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
    exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
      url: process.env.OTLP_METRICS_ENDPOINT || 'http://prometheus:9090/api/v1/otlp',
    }),
    exportIntervalMillis: 60000,
  });

  const sdk = new NodeSDK({
    resource,
    traceExporter,
    metricReader,
    instrumentations: [
      getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
        '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-fs': {
          enabled: false,
        },
      }),
      new WinstonInstrumentation({
        logHook: (span, record) => {
          record['service.name'] = serviceName;
          record['trace_id'] = span.spanContext().traceId;
          record['span_id'] = span.spanContext().spanId;
        },
      }),
      new ExpressInstrumentation(),
      new HttpInstrumentation(),
    ],
  });

  sdk.start();

  process.on('SIGTERM', async () => {
    try {
      await sdk.shutdown();
      logger.info('OpenTelemetry SDK shut down successfully');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Error shutting down OpenTelemetry SDK:', error);
    }
  });

  return sdk;
}

// Middleware para tracing de requests
import { trace } from '@opentelemetry/api';

export function traceMiddleware(req: any, res: any, next: any): void {
  const tracer = trace.getTracer('http');
  const span = tracer.startSpan(`${req.method} ${req.path}`);
  
  // Adicionar atributos ao span
  span.setAttributes({
    'http.method': req.method,
    'http.url': req.url,
    'http.route': req.path,
    'http.host': req.headers.host,
    'http.user_agent': req.headers['user-agent'],
  });

  // Propagar trace ID para logs
  const spanContext = span.spanContext();
  req.traceId = spanContext.traceId;
  req.spanId = spanContext.spanId;

  // Finalizar span quando response terminar
  res.on('finish', () => {
    span.setAttribute('http.status_code', res.statusCode);
    span.end();
  });

  next();
}
```

## 6. Diagrama de Sequência - Fluxo Crítico (Processamento de Pedido)

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant C as Cliente (Frontend)
    participant API as API Gateway
    participant A as Auth Service
    participant O as Order Service
    participant P as Payment Service
    participant Q as Queue Service
    participant N as Notification Service
    participant DB as PostgreSQL
    participant Cache as Redis
    participant Monitor as OpenTelemetry

    Note over C,Monitor: Fluxo: Criar Pedido com Pagamento
    
    C->>API: POST /api/orders (com token)
    API->>A: Validar token JWT
    A-->>API: Token válido (user_id)
    
    API->>Monitor: Iniciar trace "create_order"
    API->>O: Criar pedido (com user_id)
    
    O->>DB: Iniciar transação
    O->>DB: Inserir pedido
    O->>Cache: Cache miss - buscar produtos
    Cache-->>O: Dados

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO DIYAPP V12 CORE
# src/
# ├── services/
# │   ├── user_service/
# │   ├── task_orchestrator/
# │   └── analytics_service/
# ├── core/
# │   ├── security/
# │   ├── database/
# │   └── middleware/
# ├── api/
# └── public/

# 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO PRINCIPAL
# src/config.py
import os
from datetime import timedelta
from typing import Dict, Any
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass
from functools import lru_cache

@dataclass
class DatabaseConfig:
    url: str = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp")
    pool_size: int = int(os.getenv("DB_POOL_SIZE", "20"))
    max_overflow: int = int(os.getenv("DB_MAX_OVERFLOW", "40"))
    pool_timeout: int = int(os.getenv("DB_POOL_TIMEOUT", "30"))
    echo: bool = os.getenv("DB_ECHO", "false").lower() == "true"

@dataclass
class JWTAuthConfig:
    secret_key: str = os.getenv("JWT_SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production")
    algorithm: str = "HS256"
    access_token_expire_minutes: int = int(os.getenv("JWT_ACCESS_EXPIRE", "30"))
    refresh_token_expire_days: int = int(os.getenv("JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRE", "7"))
    
@dataclass
class OAuth2Config:
    google_client_id: str = os.getenv("GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID", "")
    google_client_secret: str = os.getenv("GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET", "")
    github_client_id: str = os.getenv("GITHUB_CLIENT_ID", "")
    github_client_secret: str = os.getenv("GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET", "")
    redirect_base_url: str = os.getenv("OAUTH_REDIRECT_URL", "http://localhost:8000")
    
@dataclass
class AnalyticsConfig:
    events_buffer_size: int = int(os.getenv("ANALYTICS_BUFFER_SIZE", "1000"))
    flush_interval_seconds: int = int(os.getenv("ANALYTICS_FLUSH_INTERVAL", "60"))
    enable_realtime: bool = os.getenv("ANALYTICS_REALTIME", "true").lower() == "true"
    
@dataclass
class TaskOrchestratorConfig:
    max_concurrent_workflows: int = int(os.getenv("MAX_CONCURRENT_WORKFLOWS", "100"))
    workflow_timeout_seconds: int = int(os.getenv("WORKFLOW_TIMEOUT", "3600"))
    retry_max_attempts: int = int(os.getenv("WORKFLOW_RETRY_ATTEMPTS", "3"))
    retry_backoff_factor: float = float(os.getenv("WORKFLOW_RETRY_BACKOFF", "1.5"))
    
@dataclass
class AppConfig:
    debug: bool = os.getenv("DEBUG", "false").lower() == "true"
    environment: str = os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT", "development")
    cors_origins: list = os.getenv("CORS_ORIGINS", "http://localhost:3000").split(",")
    rate_limit_requests: int = int(os.getenv("RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS", "100"))
    rate_limit_window: int = int(os.getenv("RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW", "60"))
    
    database: DatabaseConfig = DatabaseConfig()
    jwt_auth: JWTAuthConfig = JWTAuthConfig()
    oauth2: OAuth2Config = OAuth2Config()
    analytics: AnalyticsConfig = AnalyticsConfig()
    task_orchestrator: TaskOrchestratorConfig = TaskOrchestratorConfig()
    
@lru_cache()
def get_config() -> AppConfig:
    return AppConfig()

# 2. CORE - SEGURANÇA E AUTENTICAÇÃO
# src/core/security/auth.py
import jwt
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from fastapi import HTTPException, status, Depends
from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
from passlib.context import CryptContext
import uuid
import hashlib

class SecurityException(HTTPException):
    def __init__(self, detail: str, status_code: int = status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED):
        super().__init__(status_code=status_code, detail=detail)

class AuthService:
    def __init__(self, config: AppConfig):
        self.config = config
        self.pwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")
        self.security = HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)
        
    def verify_password(self, plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
        """Verifica senha com bcrypt"""
        try:
            return self.pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)
        except Exception:
            # Log mas não expõe detalhes
            logging.warning("Password verification failed")
            return False
    
    def get_password_hash(self, password: str) -> str:
        """Gera hash bcrypt da senha"""
        return self.pwd_context.hash(password)
    
    def create_access_token(self, data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
        """Cria JWT access token"""
        to_encode = data.copy()
        
        if expires_delta:
            expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta
        else:
            expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=self.config.jwt_auth.access_token_expire_minutes)
            
        to_encode.update({
            "exp": expire,
            "iat": datetime.utcnow(),
            "type": "access",
            "jti": str(uuid.uuid4())  # ID único para token
        })
        
        encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(
            to_encode, 
            self.config.jwt_auth.secret_key, 
            algorithm=self.config.jwt_auth.algorithm
        )
        return encoded_jwt
    
    def create_refresh_token(self, user_id: str) -> str:
        """Cria JWT refresh token"""
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=self.config.jwt_auth.refresh_token_expire_days)
        
        to_encode = {
            "sub": user_id,
            "exp": expire,
            "iat": datetime.utcnow(),
            "type": "refresh",
            "jti": str(uuid.uuid4())
        }
        
        encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(
            to_encode,
            self.config.jwt_auth.secret_key,
            algorithm=self.config.jwt_auth.algorithm
        )
        return encoded_jwt
    
    def verify_token(self, token: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Verifica e decodifica JWT token"""
        try:
            payload = jwt.decode(
                token,
                self.config.jwt_auth.secret_key,
                algorithms=[self.config.jwt_auth.algorithm]
            )
            return payload
        except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:
            raise SecurityException("Token has expired")
        except jwt.InvalidTokenError as e:
            logging.warning(f"Invalid token: {str(e)}")
            raise SecurityException("Invalid token")
    
    def generate_idempotency_key(self, user_id: str, operation: str, payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """Gera chave idempotente única para operação"""
        payload_str = str(sorted(payload.items()))
        hash_input = f"{user_id}:{operation}:{payload_str}"
        return hashlib.sha256(hash_input.encode()).hexdigest()

# 3. CORE - MIDDLEWARE E RESILIÊNCIA
# src/core/middleware/resilience.py
import time
from typing import Callable, Any, Optional
from functools import wraps
import asyncio
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import redis
from redis.exceptions import RedisError

class CircuitBreakerException(Exception):
    pass

class ResilienceMiddleware:
    def __init__(self, redis_client: Optional[redis.Redis] = None):
        self.redis = redis_client
        
    def circuit_breaker(self, failure_threshold: int = 5, recovery_timeout: int = 60):
        """Decorator para circuit breaker"""
        def decorator(func: Callable):
            @circuit(failure_threshold=failure_threshold, recovery_timeout=recovery_timeout)
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    return await func(*args, **kwargs)
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Circuit breaker caught exception in {func.__name__}: {str(e)}")
                    raise CircuitBreakerException(f"Service temporarily unavailable: {func.__name__}")
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    def retry_with_backoff(self, max_retries: int = 3, base_delay: float = 1.0):
        """Decorator para retry com backoff exponencial + jitter"""
        def decorator(func: Callable):
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                last_exception = None
                
                for attempt in range(max_retries + 1):
                    try:
                        return await func(*args, **kwargs)
                    except Exception as e:
                        last_exception = e
                        
                        # Não retry para erros 4xx (exceto 429)
                        if hasattr(e, 'status_code') and 400 <= e.status_code < 500 and e.status_code != 429:
                            raise
                        
                        if attempt == max_retries:
                            break
                            
                        # Backoff exponencial + jitter
                        delay = base_delay * (2 ** attempt)
                        jitter = delay * 0.1  # 10% jitter
                        actual_delay = delay + (jitter * (2 * (time.time() % 1) - 1))
                        
                        logging.warning(
                            f"Retry attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries} for {func.__name__} "
                            f"after {actual_delay:.2f}s. Error: {str(e)}"
                        )
                        
                        await asyncio.sleep(actual_delay)
                
                raise last_exception
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    def timeout(self, timeout_seconds: float):
        """Decorator para timeout explícito"""
        def decorator(func: Callable):
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                try:
                    return await asyncio.wait_for(
                        func(*args, **kwargs),
                        timeout=timeout_seconds
                    )
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    logging.error(f"Timeout after {timeout_seconds}s in {func.__name__}")
                    raise TimeoutError(f"Operation timed out after {timeout_seconds} seconds")
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    async def get_idempotency_result(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """Recupera resultado de operação idempotente"""
        if not self.redis:
            return None
            
        try:
            result = self.redis.get(f"idempotency:{key}")
            return result.decode() if result else None
        except RedisError as e:
            logging.error(f"Redis error in idempotency check: {str(e)}")
            return None
    
    async def set_idempotency_result(self, key: str, result: Any, ttl: int = 86400):
        """Armazena resultado de operação idempotente (24h default)"""
        if not self.redis:
            return
            
        try:
            self.redis.setex(f"idempotency:{key}", ttl, str(result))
        except RedisError as e:
            logging.error(f"Redis error storing idempotency result: {str(e)}")

# 4. USER SERVICE
# src/services/user_service/service.py
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, EmailStr, validator
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Boolean, DateTime, Text, JSON
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
import uuid
from datetime import datetime

Base = declarative_base()

class UserModel(Base):
    __tablename__ = "users"
    
    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True, default=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    email = Column(String(255), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    username = Column(String(100), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    hashed_password = Column(String(255))
    full_name = Column(String(255))
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    is_verified = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)
    
    # OAuth2
    oauth_provider = Column(String(50))
    oauth_id = Column(String(255))
    oauth_data = Column(JSON)
    
    # Permissões
    roles = Column(JSON, default=list)
    permissions = Column(JSON, default=list)

class UserCreate(BaseModel):
    email: EmailStr
    username: str
    password: str
    full_name: Optional[str] = None
    
    @validator('password')
    def validate_password(cls, v):
        if len(v) < 8:
            raise ValueError('Password must be at least 8 characters')
        return v
    
    @validator('username')
    def validate_username(cls, v):
        if not v.isalnum():
            raise ValueError('Username must be alphanumeric')
        return v

class UserUpdate(BaseModel):
    full_name: Optional[str] = None
    is_active: Optional[bool] = None

class UserResponse(BaseModel):
    id: str
    email: str
    username: str
    full_name: Optional[str]
    is_active: bool
    is_verified: bool
    created_at: datetime
    roles: List[str] = []
    
    class Config:
        from_attributes = True

class TokenResponse(BaseModel):
    access_token: str
    refresh_token: str
    token_type: str = "bearer"
    expires_in: int
    user: UserResponse

class UserRepository:
    def __init__(self, db: Session):
        self.db = db
    
    def get_by_id(self, user_id: str) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Busca usuário por ID com query parametrizada"""
        return self.db.query(UserModel).filter(UserModel.id == user_id).first()
    
    def get_by_email(self, email: str) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Busca usuário por email com query parametrizada"""
        return self.db.query(UserModel).filter(UserModel.email == email).first()
    
    def get_by_username(self, username: str) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Busca usuário por username com query parametrizada"""
        return self.db.query(UserModel).filter(UserModel.username == username).first()
    
    def get_by_oauth(self, provider: str, oauth_id: str) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Busca usuário por OAuth provider e ID"""
        return self.db.query(UserModel).filter(
            UserModel.oauth_provider == provider,
            UserModel.oauth_id == oauth_id
        ).first()
    
    def create(self, user_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> UserModel:
        """Cria novo usuário"""
        user = UserModel(**user_data)
        self.db.add(user)
        self.db.commit()
        self.db.refresh(user)
        return user
    
    def update(self, user_id: str, update_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Atualiza usuário"""
        user = self.get_by_id(user_id)
        if not user:
            return None
            
        for key, value in update_data.items():
            setattr(user, key, value)
            
        user.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()
        self.db.commit()
        self.db.refresh(user)
        return user
    
    def delete(self, user_id: str) -> bool:
        """Soft delete do usuário"""
        user = self.get_by_id(user_id)
        if not user:
            return False
            
        user.is_active = False
        user.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()
        self.db.commit()
        return True

class UserService:
    def __init__(self, repository: UserRepository, auth_service: AuthService):
        self.repository = repository
        self.auth_service = auth_service
        self.resilience = ResilienceMiddleware()
    
    @ResilienceMiddleware().circuit_breaker(failure_threshold=3)
    @ResilienceMiddleware().timeout(5.0)
    async def register_user(self, user_data: UserCreate) -> UserResponse:
        """Registra novo usuário com idempotência"""
        # Verifica se usuário já existe
        existing = self.repository.get_by_email(user_data.email)
        if existing:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT,
                detail="User with this email already exists"
            )
        
        existing_username = self.repository.get_by_username(user_data.username)
        if existing_username:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT,
                detail="Username already taken"
            )
        
        # Hash da senha
        hashed_password = self.auth_service.get_password_hash(user_data.password)
        
        # Cria usuário
        user_dict = user_data.dict(exclude={'password'})
        user_dict['hashed_password'] = hashed_password
        
        user = self.repository.create(user_dict)
        
        return UserResponse.from_orm(user)
    
    @ResilienceMiddleware().circuit_breaker(failure_threshold=3)
    async def authenticate_user(self, username: str, password: str) -> Optional[UserModel]:
        """Autentica usuário com credenciais"""
        # Tenta por email primeiro, depois username
        user = self.repository.get_by_email(username)
        if not user:
            user = self.repository.get_by_

export interface User {
  id: string
  name: string
  email: string
  avatar?: string
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest'
}

export interface AppState {
  user: User | null
  theme: 'light' | 'dark'
  sidebarOpen: boolean
  isLoading: boolean
  notifications: Notification[]
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error'
  title: string
  message: string
  timestamp: Date
  read: boolean
}

export interface RouteConfig {
  path: string
  label: string
  icon: React.ComponentType
  component: React.ComponentType
  requiresAuth: boolean
}
```

## 10. src/store/index.ts

```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand'
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware'
import { AppState, User } from '../types'

interface AppStore extends AppState {
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void
  setTheme: (theme: 'light' | 'dark') => void
  toggleSidebar: () => void
  setLoading: (isLoading: boolean) => void
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void
  markNotificationAsRead: (id: string) => void
  clearNotifications: () => void
}

const initialState: AppState = {
  user: null,
  theme: 'light',
  sidebarOpen: true,
  isLoading: false,
  notifications: []
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppStore>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      ...initialState,
      
      setUser: (user) => set({ user }),
      
      setTheme: (theme) => {
        set({ theme })
        document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', theme)
      },
      
      toggleSidebar: () => set((state) => ({ sidebarOpen: !state.sidebarOpen })),
      
      setLoading: (isLoading) => set({ isLoading }),
      
      addNotification: (notification) => {
        const newNotification = {
          ...notification,
          id: crypto.randomUUID(),
          timestamp: new Date(),
          read: false
        }
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: [newNotification, ...state.notifications].slice(0, 50)
        }))
      },
      
      markNotificationAsRead: (id) => {
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.map((n) =>
            n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n
          )
        }))
      },
      
      clearNotifications: () => set({ notifications: [] })
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        user: state.user,
        theme: state.theme,
        sidebarOpen: state.sidebarOpen
      })
    }
  )
)
```

## 11. src/routes/index.tsx

```typescript
import { Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { lazy, Suspense } from 'react'
import { useAppStore } from '../store'
import { Home } from './Home'
import { Dashboard } from './Dashboard'
import { Settings } from './Settings'

const LazyComponent = ({ component: Component }: { component: React.ComponentType }) => (
  <Suspense fallback={<div className="loading-spinner">Carregando...</div>}>
    <Component />
  </Suspense>
)

export const AppRoutes = () => {
  const { user } = useAppStore()

  return (
    <Routes>
      <Route path="/" element={<Home />} />
      <Route 
        path="/dashboard" 
        element={user ? <Dashboard /> : <Navigate to="/" replace />} 
      />
      <Route 
        path="/settings" 
        element={user ? <Settings /> : <Navigate to="/" replace />} 
      />
      <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
    </Routes>
  )
}
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
Para este projeto, abordarei a tarefa específica de criar um esquema de dados para eventos de usuário e configurar um pipeline de ingestão. A ingestão será feita utilizando Kafka para a coleta de eventos de telemetria e Vector para o roteamento dos logs, além de criar as views materializadas necessárias usando um data warehouse, como BigQuery. Vamos prosseguir com as etapas detalhadas:

### 1. Definir o Esquema de Dados para Eventos de Usuário

Usaremos o Avro para definir nosso schema de eventos devido à sua eficiência de serialização e compatibilidade com Kafka. O JSON Schema também pode ser usado para validação.

#### Esquema em Avro
```json
{
  "type": "record",
  "name": "UserEvent",
  "namespace": "com.diyapp.events",
  "fields": [
    {"name": "event_id", "type": "string"},
    {"name": "user_id", "type": "string"},
    {"name": "event_type", "type": "string"},
    {"name": "timestamp", "type": "long"},
    {"name": "properties", "type": {"type": "map", "values": "string"}}
  ]
}
```

#### Esquema em JSON Schema
```json
{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-07/schema#",
  "title": "UserEvent",
  "type": "object",
  "properties": {
    "event_id": {
      "type": "string"
    },
    "user_id": {
      "type": "string"
    },
    "event_type": {
      "type": "string"
    },
    "timestamp": {
      "type": "integer"
    },
    "properties": {
      "type": "object",
      "additionalProperties": {
        "type": "string"
      }
    }
  },
  "required": ["event_id", "user_id", "event_type", "timestamp"]
}
```

### 2. Configuração do Pipeline de Ingestão

#### Kafka Producer para Enviar Eventos
```python
from confluent_kafka import Producer
import json
import time

def delivery_report(err, msg):
    if err is not None:
        print(f"Message delivery failed: {err}")
    else:
        print(f"Message delivered to {msg.topic()} [{msg.partition()}]")

p = Producer({'bootstrap.servers': 'localhost:9092'})

event = {
    "event_id": "abcd1234",
    "user_id": "user_5678",
    "event_type": "purchase",
    "timestamp": int(time.time() * 1000),
    "properties": {
        "product_id": "prod_1234",
        "price": "29.99"
    }
}

p.produce('user-events', key=event['event_id'], value=json.dumps(event), callback=delivery_report)
p.flush()
```

#### Vector Configuration for Log Roteamento
Create a `vector.toml` file for configuration:
```toml
[sources.my_source]
  type = "kafka"
  bootstrap_servers = "localhost:9092"
  topics = ["user-events"]
  group_id = "vector_group"

[sinks.my_sink]
  type = "console"
  inputs = ["my_source"]
  encoding.codec = "json"
  print_time = true
```

### 3. Criando Views Materializadas no BigQuery

Assumindo que os dados já são ingeridos no BigQuery em uma tabela chamada `raw_user_events`, podemos criar uma view materializada:

```sql
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW IF NOT EXISTS diyapp_analytics.perf_dashboard AS
SELECT
  user_id,
  event_type,
  COUNT(*) AS event_count,
  MAX(timestamp) AS last_event_time
FROM
  diyapp_events.raw_user_events
GROUP BY
  user_id, event_type;
```

### Estrutura de Arquivos

```
/diyapp-evolution/
│
├── src/
│   ├── producer.py         # Kafka producer script
│   └── consumer.py         # Example for future extension
├── public/
│   └── index.html          # For UI Dashboard Connection (future work)
└── config/
    ├── avro_schema.avsc    # Avro schema for Kafka
    ├── json_schema.json    # JSON schema for validation
    └── vector.toml         # Vector configuration
```

Para completar a instalação, certifique-se de ter o Kafka, Vector e BigQuery configurados. O Kafka deve estar rodando localmente ou em um ambiente acessível, e o Google Cloud SDK deve estar configurado para acessar o BigQuery.

Essa implementação completa a configuração básica de um pipeline de ingestão com Kafka e Vector, e a primeira etapa de análise com uma view materializada no BigQuery. Ajustes adicionais podem ser feitos conforme as especificações do projeto avançarem.

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# Terraform Infrastructure for DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core (Staging)

Vou provisionar a infraestrutura como código para o ambiente de staging, seguindo as melhores práticas de SRE para confiabilidade e observabilidade. O código será modular, com variáveis para fácil adaptação entre AWS (EKS) e GCP (GKE).

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
/terraform-staging
├── modules/
│   ├── networking/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── outputs.tf
│   │   └── variables.tf
│   ├── kubernetes/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── outputs.tf
│   │   └── variables.tf
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── outputs.tf
│   │   └── variables.tf
│   └── monitoring/
│       ├── main.tf
│       ├── outputs.tf
│       └── variables.tf
├── environments/
│   └── staging/
│       ├── main.tf
│       ├── outputs.tf
│       ├── variables.tf
│       └── terraform.tfvars
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
│       ├── terraform-plan.yml
│       └── terraform-apply.yml
└── README.md
```

## 1. Módulo de Networking (VPC)

```hcl
# modules/networking/variables.tf
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name (staging, production)"
  type        = string
}

variable "region" {
  description = "AWS/GCP region"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for VPC"
  type        = string
}

variable "public_subnets" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "private_subnets" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  type        = string
}

# modules/networking/main.tf
locals {
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Terraform   = "true"
    Squad       = "Autonomous Senior Squad"
  }
}

# AWS VPC Configuration
resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  count                = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_support   = true
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  tags                 = merge(local.tags, { Name = "${var.environment}-vpc" })
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count                   = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? length(var.public_subnets) : 0
  vpc_id                  = aws_vpc.main[0].id
  cidr_block              = var.public_subnets[count.index]
  availability_zone       = "${var.region}${element(["a", "b", "c"], count.index)}"
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true
  tags                    = merge(local.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-public-${count.index}",
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
  })
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? length(var.private_subnets) : 0
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main[0].id
  cidr_block        = var.private_subnets[count.index]
  availability_zone = "${var.region}${element(["a", "b", "c"], count.index)}"
  tags              = merge(local.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-private-${count.index}",
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
  })
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "gw" {
  count  = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main[0].id
  tags   = merge(local.tags, { Name = "${var.environment}-igw" })
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  count  = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main[0].id
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.gw[0].id
  }
  tags = merge(local.tags, { Name = "${var.environment}-public-rt" })
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? length(var.public_subnets) : 0
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public[0].id
}

# GCP VPC Configuration
resource "google_compute_network" "vpc" {
  count                   = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  name                    = "${var.environment}-vpc"
  auto_create_subnetworks = false
  routing_mode            = "REGIONAL"
}

resource "google_compute_subnetwork" "public" {
  count         = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? length(var.public_subnets) : 0
  name          = "${var.environment}-public-${count.index}"
  ip_cidr_range = var.public_subnets[count.index]
  region        = var.region
  network       = google_compute_network.vpc[0].id
  private_ip_google_access = true
}

resource "google_compute_subnetwork" "private" {
  count         = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? length(var.private_subnets) : 0
  name          = "${var.environment}-private-${count.index}"
  ip_cidr_range = var.private_subnets[count.index]
  region        = var.region
  network       = google_compute_network.vpc[0].id
  private_ip_google_access = true
}

# modules/networking/outputs.tf
output "vpc_id" {
  description = "The ID of the VPC"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_vpc.main[0].id : google_compute_network.vpc[0].id
}

output "public_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of public subnet IDs"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_subnet.public[*].id : google_compute_subnetwork.public[*].id
}

output "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of private subnet IDs"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_subnet.private[*].id : google_compute_subnetwork.private[*].id
}

output "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "The CIDR block of the VPC"
  value       = var.vpc_cidr
}
```

## 2. Módulo Kubernetes (EKS/GKE)

```hcl
# modules/kubernetes/variables.tf
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  type        = string
}

variable "region" {
  description = "AWS/GCP region"
  type        = string
}

variable "cloud_provider" {
  description = "Cloud provider (aws or gcp)"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_id" {
  description = "VPC ID"
  type        = string
}

variable "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of private subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "public_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of public subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "node_groups" {
  description = "Map of node groups configurations"
  type = map(object({
    min_size     = number
    max_size     = number
    desired_size = number
    instance_type = string
    disk_size    = number
  }))
}

variable "enable_autoscaling" {
  description = "Enable cluster autoscaler"
  type        = bool
  default     = true
}

# modules/kubernetes/main.tf
locals {
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Terraform   = "true"
    Squad       = "Autonomous Senior Squad"
  }
}

# AWS EKS Configuration
resource "aws_eks_cluster" "cluster" {
  count    = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name     = "${var.environment}-${var.cluster_name}"
  role_arn = aws_iam_role.eks_cluster[0].arn
  version  = "1.27"

  vpc_config {
    subnet_ids = concat(var.private_subnet_ids, var.public_subnet_ids)
  }

  depends_on = [
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.eks_cluster_policy
  ]

  tags = local.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "eks_cluster" {
  count = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name  = "${var.environment}-eks-cluster-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "eks.amazonaws.com"
        }
      }
    ]
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "eks_cluster_policy" {
  count      = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSClusterPolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.eks_cluster[0].name
}

resource "aws_eks_node_group" "nodes" {
  for_each        = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? var.node_groups : {}
  cluster_name    = aws_eks_cluster.cluster[0].name
  node_group_name = "${var.environment}-${each.key}"
  node_role_arn   = aws_iam_role.eks_nodes[0].arn
  subnet_ids      = var.private_subnet_ids

  scaling_config {
    desired_size = each.value.desired_size
    max_size     = each.value.max_size
    min_size     = each.value.min_size
  }

  instance_types = [each.value.instance_type]
  disk_size      = each.value.disk_size

  depends_on = [
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.eks_worker_node_policy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.eks_cni_policy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.ec2_container_registry_read_only,
  ]

  tags = merge(local.tags, {
    Name = "${var.environment}-${each.key}"
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "eks_nodes" {
  count = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name  = "${var.environment}-eks-nodes-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRole"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "ec2.amazonaws.com"
        }
      }
    ]
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "eks_worker_node_policy" {
  count      = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.eks_nodes[0].name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "eks_cni_policy" {
  count      = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.eks_nodes[0].name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "ec2_container_registry_read_only" {
  count      = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly"
  role       = aws_iam_role.eks_nodes[0].name
}

# GCP GKE Configuration
resource "google_container_cluster" "cluster" {
  count    = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  name     = "${var.environment}-${var.cluster_name}"
  location = var.region
  network    = var.vpc_id
  subnetwork = var.private_subnet_ids[0]

  # We can't create a cluster with no node pool defined, but we want to only use
  # separately managed node pools. So we create the smallest possible default
  # node pool and immediately delete it.
  remove_default_node_pool = true
  initial_node_count       = 1

  release_channel {
    channel = "REGULAR"
  }

  workload_identity_config {
    workload_pool = "${data.google_project.project.project_id}.svc.id.goog"
  }

  addons_config {
    horizontal_pod_autoscaling {
      disabled = false
    }
    http_load_balancing {
      disabled = false
    }
  }

  monitoring_config {
    enable_components = ["SYSTEM_COMPONENTS", "WORKLOADS"]
  }

  logging_config {
    enable_components = ["SYSTEM_COMPONENTS", "WORKLOADS"]
  }

  maintenance_policy {
    recurring_window {
      start_time = "03:00"
      end_time   = "05:00"
      recurrence = "FREQ=WEEKLY;BYDAY=SA,SU"
    }
  }
}

resource "google_container_node_pool" "nodes" {
  for_each   = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? var.node_groups : {}
  name       = "${var.environment}-${each.key}"
  location   = var.region
  cluster    = google_container_cluster.cluster[0].name
  node_count = each.value.desired_size

  autoscaling {
    min_node_count = each.value.min_size
    max_node_count = each.value.max_size
  }

  node_config {
    preemptible  = false
    machine_type = each.value.instance_type
    disk_size_gb = each.value.disk_size
    disk_type    = "pd-standard"
    oauth_scopes = [
      "https://www.googleapis.com/auth/cloud-platform"
    ]

    workload_metadata_config {
      mode = "GKE_METADATA"
    }
  }

  management {
    auto_repair  = true
    auto_upgrade = true
  }
}

data "google_project" "project" {
  count = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
}

# modules/kubernetes/outputs.tf
output "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_eks_cluster.cluster[0].name : google_container_cluster.cluster[0].name
}

output "cluster_endpoint" {
  description = "Endpoint for EKS/GKE control plane"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_eks_cluster.cluster[0].endpoint : google_container_cluster.cluster[0].endpoint
}

output "cluster_ca_certificate" {
  description = "Base64 encoded CA certificate"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_eks_cluster.cluster[0].certificate_authority[0].data : google_container_cluster.cluster[0].master_auth[0].cluster_ca_certificate
  sensitive   = true
}

output "cluster_token" {
  description = "Cluster authentication token"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster[0].token : data.google_client_config.default.access_token
  sensitive   = true
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "cluster" {
  count    = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name     = aws_eks_cluster.cluster[0].name
}

data "google_client_config" "default" {
  count = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
}
```

## 3. Módulo de Banco de Dados

```hcl
# modules/database/variables.tf
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
}

variable "region" {
  description = "AWS/GCP region"
  type        = string
}

variable "cloud_provider" {
  description = "Cloud provider (aws or gcp)"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_id" {
  description = "VPC ID"
  type        = string
}

variable "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of private subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

variable "database_name" {
  description = "Database name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp"
}

variable "database_username" {
  description = "Database admin username"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp_admin"
}

variable "database_password" {
  description = "Database admin password"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "database_instance_class" {
  description = "Database instance class"
  type        = string
  default     = "db.t3.medium"
}

variable "database_allocated_storage" {
  description = "Allocated storage in GB"
  type        = number
  default     = 20
}

variable "database_engine" {
  description = "Database engine"
  type        = string
  default     = "postgres"
}

variable "database_engine_version" {
  description = "Database engine version"
  type        = string
  default     = "13.4"
}

# modules/database/main.tf
locals {
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Terraform   = "true"
    Squad       = "Autonomous Senior Squad"
  }
}

# AWS RDS Configuration
resource "aws_db_subnet_group" "db_subnet" {
  count       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name        = "${var.environment}-db-subnet-group"
  description = "Database subnet group for ${var.environment}"
  subnet_ids  = var.private_subnet_ids
  tags        = local.tags
}

resource "aws_db_instance" "database" {
  count                  = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  identifier             = "${var.environment}-${var.database_name}"
  engine                 = var.database_engine
  engine_version         = var.database_engine_version
  instance_class         = var.database_instance_class
  allocated_storage      = var.database_allocated_storage
  max_allocated_storage  = var.database_allocated_storage * 2
  storage_type           = "gp2"
  db_name                = var.database_name
  username               = var.database_username
  password               = var.database_password
  parameter_group_name   = "default.postgres13"
  skip_final_snapshot    = true
  vpc_security_group_ids = [aws_security_group.db[0].id]
  db_subnet_group_name   = aws_db_subnet_group.db_subnet[0].name
  multi_az               = true
  publicly_accessible    = false
  storage_encrypted      = true
  backup_retention_period = 7
  deletion_protection    = true

  tags = local.tags
}

resource "aws_security_group" "db" {
  count       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name        = "${var.environment}-db-sg"
  description = "Security group for database"
  vpc_id      = var.vpc_id

  ingress {
    from_port   = 5432
    to_port     = 5432
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = ["10.0.0.0/16"] # Allow from VPC only
  }

  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  tags = local.tags
}

# GCP Cloud SQL Configuration
resource "google_sql_database_instance" "database" {
  count            = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  name             = "${var.environment}-${var.database_name}"
  region           = var.region
  database_version = "POSTGRES_13"

  settings {
    tier              = "db-f1-micro"
    availability_type = "REGIONAL"
    disk_size         = var.database_allocated_storage
    disk_type         = "PD_SSD"

    ip_configuration {
      ipv4_enabled    = false
      private_network = var.vpc_id
    }

    backup_configuration {
      enabled    = true
      start_time = "03:00"
    }

    maintenance_window {
      day          = 7 # Sunday
      hour         = 3
      update_track = "stable"
    }
  }

  deletion_protection = true
}

resource "google_sql_database" "database" {
  count    = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  name     = var.database_name
  instance = google_sql_database_instance.database[0].name
}

resource "google_sql_user" "users" {
  count    = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  name     = var.database_username
  instance = google_sql_database_instance.database[0].name
  password = var.database_password
}

# modules/database/outputs.tf
output "db_instance_address" {
  description = "Database instance address"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_db_instance.database[0].address : google_sql_database_instance.database[0].private_ip_address
}

output "db_instance_endpoint" {
  description = "Database instance endpoint"
  value       = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? aws_db_instance.database[0].endpoint : "${google_sql_database_instance.database[0].private_ip_address}:5432"
}

output "db_instance_name" {
  description = "Database instance name"
  value       = var.database_name
}

output "db_instance_username" {
  description = "Database admin username"
  value       = var.database_username
  sensitive   = true
}

output "db_instance_password" {
  description = "Database admin password"
  value       = var.database_password
  sensitive   = true
}
```

## 4. Módulo de Monitoring

```hcl
# modules/monitoring/variables.tf
variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
}

variable "region" {
  description = "AWS/GCP region"
  type        = string
}

variable "cloud_provider" {
  description = "Cloud provider (aws or gcp)"
  type        = string
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  type        = string
}

variable "cluster_endpoint" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster endpoint"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_id" {
  description = "VPC ID"
  type        = string
}

variable "private_subnet_ids" {
  description = "List of private subnet IDs"
  type        = list(string)
}

# modules/monitoring/main.tf
locals {
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Terraform   = "true"
    Squad       = "Autonomous Senior Squad"
  }
}

# AWS CloudWatch Configuration
resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "eks" {
  count             = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name              = "/aws/eks/${var.environment}-${var.cluster_name}/cluster"
  retention_in_days = 30
  tags              = local.tags
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_metric_alarm" "high_cpu" {
  count               = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  alarm_name          = "${var.environment}-high-cpu-utilization"
  comparison_operator = "GreaterThanThreshold"
  evaluation_periods  = "2"
  metric_name         = "CPUUtilization"
  namespace           = "AWS/EC2"
  period              = "300"
  statistic           = "Average"
  threshold           = "80"
  alarm_description   = "This metric monitors high CPU utilization"
  alarm_actions       = [aws_sns_topic.alerts[0].arn]

  dimensions = {
    AutoScalingGroupName = "${var.environment}-nodes"
  }

  tags = local.tags
}

resource "aws_sns_topic" "alerts" {
  count = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  name  = "${var.environment}-alerts"
  tags  = local.tags
}

resource "aws_sns_topic_subscription" "email" {
  count     = var.cloud_provider == "aws" ? 1 : 0
  topic_arn = aws_sns_topic.alerts[0].arn
  protocol  = "email"
  endpoint  = "sre-team@diyapp.com"
}

# GCP Monitoring Configuration
resource "google_monitoring_notification_channel" "email" {
  count        = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  display_name = "${var.environment}-email-alerts"
  type         = "email"
  labels = {
    email_address = "sre-team@diyapp.com"
  }
}

resource "google_monitoring_alert_policy" "high_cpu" {
  count        = var.cloud_provider == "gcp" ? 1 : 0
  display_name = "${var.environment}-high-cpu-utilization"
  combiner     = "OR"

  conditions {
    display_name = "High CPU utilization"

    condition_threshold {
      filter          = "resource.type=\"k8s_container\" AND metric.type=\"kubernetes.io/container/cpu/usage_rate\""
      duration        = "300s"
      comparison      = "COMPARISON_GT"
      threshold_value = "0.8"
      aggregations {
        alignment_period   = "60s"
        per_series_aligner = "ALIGN_MEAN"
      }
    }
  }

  notification_channels = [google_monitoring_notification_channel.email[0].name]
  enabled              = true
}

# Kubernetes Monitoring with Prometheus and Grafana
resource "helm_release" "prometheus" {
  name       = "prometheus"
  repository = "https://prometheus-community.github.io/helm-charts"
  chart      = "kube-prometheus-stack"
  version    = "45.7.1"
  namespace  = "monitoring"
  create_namespace = true

  values = [
    file("${path.module}/values/prometheus-values.yaml")
  ]

  set {
    name  = "grafana.adminPassword"
    value = var.grafana_admin_password
  }

  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.serviceMonitorSelectorNilUsesHelmValues"
    value = "false"
  }

  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.podMonitorSelectorNilUsesHelmValues"
    value = "false"
  }

  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.ruleSelectorNilUsesHelmValues"
    value = "false"
  }
}

# modules/monitoring/outputs.tf
output "monitoring_dashboard_url" {
  description = "URL for the monitoring dashboard"
  value       = "https://grafana.${var.environment}.diyapp.com"
}

output "alert_manager_url" {
  description = "URL for the alert manager"
  value       = "https://alertmanager.${var.environment}.diyapp.com"
}
```

## 5. Configuração do Ambiente Staging

```hcl
# environments/staging/variables.tf
variable "region" {
  description = "AWS/GCP region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "cloud_provider" {
  description = "Cloud provider (aws or gcp)"
  type        = string
  default     = "aws"
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for VPC"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "public_subnets" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
}

variable "private_subnets" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-cluster"
}

variable "node_groups" {
  description = "Node groups configuration"
  type = map(object({
    min_size     = number
    max_size     = number
    desired_size = number
    instance_type = string
    disk_size    = number
  }))
  default = {
    "default" = {
      min_size     = 2
      max_size     = 5
      desired_size = 2
      instance_type = "t3.medium"
      disk_size    = 50
    }
    "llm" = {
      min_size     = 1
      max_size     = 3
      desired_size = 1
      instance_type = "g4dn.xlarge"
      disk_size    = 100
    }
  }
}

variable "database_password" {
  description = "Database admin password"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

variable "grafana_admin_password" {
  description = "Grafana admin password"
  type        = string
  sensitive   = true
}

# environments/staging/main.tf
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.0.0"

  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 4.0"
    }
    google = {
      source  = "hashicorp/google"
      version = "~> 4.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.0"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.0"
    }
  }

  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "staging/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-lock"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.region
}

provider "google" {
  project = "diyapp-project"
  region  = var.region
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.kubernetes.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.kubernetes.cluster_ca_certificate)
  token                  = module.kubernetes.cluster_token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.kubernetes.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.kubernetes.cluster_ca_certificate)
    token                  = module.kubernetes.cluster_token
  }
}

  vpc_id             = module.networking.vpc_id
  private_subnet_ids = module.networking.private_subnet_ids
  database_password  = var.database_password
}
