## 2. CI/CD com GitHub Actions

### .github/workflows/terraform.yml

```yaml
name: Terraform

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
    paths:
      - 'terraform/**'
  pull_request:
    paths:
      - 'terraform/**'

env:
  TF_VERSION: 1.5.7
  AWS_REGION: us-east-1

jobs:
  terraform:
    name: Terraform
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      id-token: write
      contents: read
      pull-requests: write

    steps:
      - name: Checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Configure AWS Credentials
        uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v4
        with:
          role-to-assume: arn:aws:iam::${{ secrets.AWS_ACCOUNT_ID }}:role/github-actions-terraform
          aws-region: ${{ env.AWS_REGION }}

      - name: Setup Terraform
        uses: hashicorp/setup-terraform@v2
        with:
          terraform_version: ${{ env.TF_VERSION }}

      - name: Terraform Init
        id: init
        run: terraform init
        working-directory: terraform

      - name: Terraform Validate
        id: validate
        run: terraform validate -no-color
        working-directory: terraform

      - name: Terraform Plan
        id: plan
        if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'
        run: terraform plan -no-color -input=false
        working-directory: terraform
        continue-on-error: true

      - name: Update Pull Request
        uses: actions/github-script@v6
        if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'
        env:
          PLAN: "terraform\n${{ steps.plan.outputs.stdout }}"
        with:
          github-token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          script: |
            const output = `#### Terraform Initialization ‚öôÔ∏è\`${{ steps.init.outcome }}\`
            #### Terraform Validation ü§ñ\`${{ steps.validate.outcome }}\`
            #### Terraform Plan üìñ\`${{ steps.plan.outcome }}\`

            <details><summary>Show Plan</summary>

            \`\`\`\n
            ${process.env.PLAN}
            \`\`\`

            </details>

            *Pusher: @${{ github.actor }}, Action: \`${{ github.event_name }}\`*`;

            github.rest.issues.createComment({
              issue_number: context.issue.number,
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              body: output
            })

      - name: Terraform Plan Status
        if: steps.plan.outcome == 'failure'
        run: exit 1

      - name: Terraform Apply
        if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' && github.event_name == 'push'
        run: terraform apply -auto-approve -input=false
        working-directory: terraform
```

### .github/workflows/deploy-staging.yml

```yaml
name: Deploy to Staging

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
    paths-ignore:
      - 'terraform/**'
      - '.github/workflows/terraform.yml'

env:
  AWS_REGION: us-east-1
  EKS_CLUSTER_NAME: diyapp-staging
  DOCKER_IMAGE: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCOUNT_ID }}.dkr.ecr.${{ env.AWS_REGION }}.amazonaws.com/diyapp:${{ github.sha }}

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    name: Build and Deploy
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      id-token: write
      contents: read

    steps:
      - name: Checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Configure AWS Credentials
        uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v4
        with:
          role-to-assume: arn:aws:iam::${{ secrets.AWS_ACCOUNT_ID }}:role/github-actions-deploy
          aws-region: ${{ env.AWS_REGION }}

      - name: Login to Amazon ECR
        id: login-ecr
        uses: aws-actions/amazon-ecr-login@v1

      - name: Build, tag, and push image to Amazon ECR
        run: |
          docker build -t ${{ env.DOCKER_IMAGE }} .
          docker push ${{ env.DOCKER_IMAGE }}

      - name: Install kubectl
        uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v3
        with:
          version: 'latest'

      - name: Update kubeconfig
        run: |
          aws eks --region ${{ env.AWS_REGION }} update-kubeconfig --name ${{ env.EKS_CLUSTER_NAME }}

      - name: Deploy to EKS
        run: |
          # Substituir a imagem no deployment
          kubectl set image deployment/diyapp diyapp=${{ env.DOCKER_IMAGE }} -n staging

          # Verificar rollout status
          kubectl rollout status deployment/diyapp -n staging

          # Verificar pods
          kubectl get pods -n staging
```

## 3. README.md

```markdown
# DIYAPP Staging Infrastructure

Infraestrutura como código para o ambiente de staging do DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core.

## Estrutura

- **Terraform**: Configuração completa da infraestrutura (VPC, EKS, RDS, ALB)
- **GitHub Actions**: Pipelines para provisionamento da infra e deploy da aplicação

## Pré-requisitos

1. Conta AWS com permissões adequadas
2. Terraform instalado localmente (para testes)
3. AWS CLI configurado
4. kubectl instalado
5. Docker instalado (para builds locais)

## Configuração Inicial

1. Criar bucket S3 para o estado do Terraform:
   ```bash
   aws s3api create-bucket --bucket diyapp-terraform-state --region us-east-1
   ```

2. Criar tabela DynamoDB para locks do Terraform:
   ```bash
   aws dynamodb create-table \
     --table-name diyapp-terraform-lock \
     --attribute-definitions AttributeName=LockID,AttributeType=S \
     --key-schema AttributeName=LockID,KeyType=HASH \
     --billing-mode PAY_PER_REQUEST \
     --region us-east-1
   ```

3. Configurar variáveis de ambiente no GitHub Secrets:
   - `AWS_ACCOUNT_ID`: ID da conta AWS
   - `DB_USERNAME`: Usuário do banco de dados
   - `DB_PASSWORD`: Senha do banco de dados
   - `GRAFANA_ADMIN_PASSWORD`: Senha admin do Grafana

## Como Usar

### Provisionar Infraestrutura

1. Fazer push das alterações na pasta `terraform/` para a branch `main` ou abrir um PR
2. O GitHub Actions executará o Terraform automaticamente

### Deploy da Aplicação

1. Fazer push das alterações no código da aplicação para a branch `main`
2. O GitHub Actions construirá a imagem Docker e fará deploy no cluster EKS

## Observabilidade

- **Grafana**: Acessível em `http://<ALB_DNS_NAME>/grafana`
  - Usuário: `admin`
  - Senha: Definida na variável `grafana_admin_password`

## SLOs e Monitoramento

A configuração inclui:
- Prometheus para coleta de métricas
- Grafana para visualização
- AWS Load Balancer Controller para gerenciamento de ALB

## Adaptação para GCP (GKE)

Para adaptar para GCP, substitua os módulos principais por equivalentes do GCP:

1. **VPC**: Usar `google_compute_network` e `google_compute_subnetwork`
2. **GKE**: Usar `google_container_cluster`
3. **RDS**: Usar `google_sql_database_instance`
4. **ALB**: Usar `google_compute_global_forwarding_rule` e `google_compute_target_http_proxy`

## Contato

Em caso de incidentes ou dúvidas, contatar o SRE da squad.
```

## Considerações Finais

1. **Segurança**:
   - As credenciais são gerenciadas via OIDC no GitHub Actions
   - O banco de dados está em subnets privadas
   - O ALB tem redirecionamento HTTP → HTTPS

2. **Observabilidade**:
   - Prometheus e Grafana estão configurados por padrão
   - O ALB expõe o Grafana na rota `/grafana`

3. **Escalabilidade**:
   - O EKS está configurado com node groups que podem escalar automaticamente
   - O RDS está configurado com Multi-AZ para alta disponibilidade

4. **Error Budget**:
   - A infraestrutura está preparada para monitorar os SLOs definidos
   - O Prometheus pode ser configurado para alertar quando os SLOs estiverem em risco

5. **Modo Hive**:
   - A estrutura permite refatoração paralela com branches separadas
   - O Terraform está modularizado para facilitar mudanças incrementais

Para implementar completamente, será necessário:
1. Criar os recursos iniciais (bucket S3 e tabela DynamoDB)
2. Configurar as variáveis no GitHub Secrets
3. Criar os IAM Roles para o GitHub Actions
4. Configurar o certificado ACM para o ALB

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
Para realizar threat modeling da arquitetura V12, definiremos políticas de IAM mínimas, configuraremos o WAF no load balancer e implementaremos sanitização de inputs no framework backend. Além disso, estabeleceremos um padrão para logging seguro. Vamos abordar essas tarefas de forma organizada.

### Threat Modeling
Usaremos o framework STRIDE para conduzir o threat modeling na arquitetura V12:

1. **Spoofing:**
   - Implementar autenticação robusta com MFA (Multi-Factor Authentication) para acesso administrativo.
   - Utilizar tokens com expiração curta e invalidação no logout.

2. **Tampering:**
   - Habilitar assinatura de payloads e verificar integridade nos dados in-transit.
   - Controlar acesso a operações críticas por meio de autorização granular.

3. **Repudiation:**
   - Implementar logs imutáveis e auditáveis para rastrear ações críticas do sistema.

4. **Information Disclosure:**
   - Assegurar que dados sensíveis estejam criptografados (AES-256) e mascarados em logs.
   - Garantir que TLS 1.2+ seja usado em todas as comunicações.

5. **Denial of Service:**
   - Configurar rate limiting e circuit breakers nas APIs para prevenir sobrecargas.
   - Monitorar e mitigar picos de carga com WAF no load balancer.

6. **Elevation of Privilege:**
   - Verificar permissões detalhadas para cada recurso usando o princípio do menor privilégio.
   - Realizar auditoria regular dos papéis e permissões atribuídos.

### Políticas de IAM Mínimas

```yaml
# IAM Policy Template
IAM:
  Users:
    - UserName: AdminUser
      Policy: AdminPolicy
      Actions: ['*']
      Resources: ['*']
  Roles:
    - RoleName: WebAppRole
      Policy: WebAppPolicy
      Actions: ['s3:GetObject', 'dynamodb:Query']
      Resources: ['arn:aws:s3:::example-bucket/*', 'arn:aws:dynamodb:us-east-1:123456789012:table/MyTable']
  MFA:
    Required: true
    Devices: ['MFADevice1']
```

### Configuração de WAF no Load Balancer

```json
# CloudFormation Template for WAF
{
  "Resources": {
    "WebACL": {
      "Type": "AWS::WAFv2::WebACL",
      "Properties": {
        "Scope": "REGIONAL",
        "DefaultAction": { "Allow": {} },
        "Rules": [
          {
            "Name": "RateLimitRule",
            "Priority": 0,
            "Action": { "Block": {} },
            "Statement": {
              "RateBasedStatement": {
                "Limit": 2000,
                "AggregateKeyType": "IP"
              }
            },
            "VisibilityConfig": {
              "SampledRequestsEnabled": true,
              "CloudWatchMetricsEnabled": true,
              "MetricName": "RateLimitRule"
            }
          }
        ],
        "VisibilityConfig": {
          "SampledRequestsEnabled": true,
          "CloudWatchMetricsEnabled": true,
          "MetricName": "WebACL"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### Sanitização de Inputs no Framework Backend
No backend (por exemplo, usando Express.js):

```javascript
// Input Sanitization Example with Express.js
const express = require('express');
const bodyParser = require('body-parser');
const xssFilters = require('xss-filters');
const app = express();

app.use(bodyParser.json());

function sanitizeInput(req, res, next) {
  for (let prop in req.body) {
    if (typeof req.body[prop] === 'string') {
      req.body[prop] = xssFilters.inHTMLData(req.body[prop]);
    }
  }
  next();
}

app.use(sanitizeInput);

app.post('/submit', (req, res) => {
  // handle the request
  res.send('Data processed safely.');
});

app.listen(3000, () => {
  console.log('Server running on port 3000');
});
```

### Padrão para Logging sem Dados Sensíveis

```javascript
const pino = require('pino');

const logger = pino({
  redact: ['req.headers.authorization', 'req.body.password'],
  level: 'info',
});

module.exports = logger;

// Usage
const logger = require('./logger');
logger.info('Server started');
logger.error('An error occurred', { errorDetails: 'Error details' });
```

Este conjunto de medidas garante que a arquitetura V12 seja estruturada com segurança desde o início, conforme as melhores práticas.

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
# Plano de Teste E2E para Fluxo Crítico de Onboarding (DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core)

## 1. Estratégia de Teste E2E

**Objetivo**: Validar o fluxo crítico completo de onboarding até a primeira tarefa criada, garantindo:
- Funcionalidade correta em todos os passos
- Performance dentro dos limites especificados (LCP < 2.5s, FID < 100ms)
- Resiliência a falhas comuns
- Consistência visual e de UX

**Escopo**:
- Teste do caminho feliz (usuário novo completando onboarding)
- Teste de recuperação de erros (falhas de rede, validações)
- Teste de performance (métricas Core Web Vitals)
- Teste de acessibilidade básica

**Ferramentas**:
- Playwright (com suporte a múltiplos browsers)
- Lighthouse (para métricas de performance)
- Faker.js (para dados sintéticos)
- Mock Service Worker (para simular APIs)

## 2. Configuração do Ambiente de Teste

### Estrutura de Diretórios
```
/tests
  /e2e
    /onboarding
      onboarding.spec.ts
      performance.spec.ts
      accessibility.spec.ts
    /fixtures
      users.ts
      tasks.ts
    /pages
      OnboardingPage.ts
      DashboardPage.ts
      TaskPage.ts
  /data
    synthetic-data.json
  playwright.config.ts
  package.json
```

### Configuração do Playwright (`playwright.config.ts`)

```typescript
import { defineConfig, devices } from '@playwright/test';

export default defineConfig({
  testDir: './tests/e2e',
  timeout: 30000,
  expect: {
    timeout: 5000
  },
  fullyParallel: true,
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 1 : undefined,
  reporter: [
    ['list'],
    ['html', { outputFolder: 'test-results' }],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'test-results/results.json' }]
  ],
  use: {
    baseURL: 'http://localhost:3000',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',
    video: 'retain-on-failure',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
  },
  projects: [
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Chrome',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Safari',
      use: { ...devices['iPhone 12'] },
    },
  ],
  webServer: {
    command: 'npm run start',
    url: 'http://localhost:3000',
    reuseExistingServer: !process.env.CI,
  },
});
```

## 3. Dados Sintéticos (`/tests/e2e/fixtures/users.ts`)

```typescript
import { faker } from '@faker-js/faker';

export const generateTestUser = () => ({
  email: faker.internet.email(),
  password: faker.internet.password({ length: 12 }),
  firstName: faker.person.firstName(),
  lastName: faker.person.lastName(),
  company: faker.company.name(),
  role: faker.helpers.arrayElement(['Developer', 'Designer', 'Product Manager', 'QA']),
  timezone: faker.location.timeZone(),
});

export const generateTestTask = () => ({
  title: faker.lorem.words(3),
  description: faker.lorem.sentences(2),
  priority: faker.helpers.arrayElement(['Low', 'Medium', 'High']),
  dueDate: faker.date.future().toISOString().split('T')[0],
});
```

## 4. Page Objects (`/tests/e2e/pages/OnboardingPage.ts`)

```typescript
import { Locator, Page } from '@playwright/test';

export class OnboardingPage {
  readonly page: Page;
  readonly emailInput: Locator;
  readonly passwordInput: Locator;
  readonly firstNameInput: Locator;
  readonly lastNameInput: Locator;
  readonly companyInput: Locator;
  readonly roleSelect: Locator;
  readonly timezoneSelect: Locator;
  readonly nextButton: Locator;
  readonly submitButton: Locator;
  readonly errorMessage: Locator;

  constructor(page: Page) {
    this.page = page;
    this.emailInput = page.getByLabel('Email');
    this.passwordInput = page.getByLabel('Password');
    this.firstNameInput = page.getByLabel('First Name');
    this.lastNameInput = page.getByLabel('Last Name');
    this.companyInput = page.getByLabel('Company');
    this.roleSelect = page.getByLabel('Role');
    this.timezoneSelect = page.getByLabel('Timezone');
    this.nextButton = page.getByRole('button', { name: 'Next' });
    this.submitButton = page.getByRole('button', { name: 'Complete Onboarding' });
    this.errorMessage = page.getByRole('alert');
  }

  async navigate() {
    await this.page.goto('/onboarding');
  }

  async fillStep1(user: { email: string; password: string }) {
    await this.emailInput.fill(user.email);
    await this.passwordInput.fill(user.password);
    await this.nextButton.click();
  }

  async fillStep2(user: { firstName: string; lastName: string; company: string }) {
    await this.firstNameInput.fill(user.firstName);
    await this.lastNameInput.fill(user.lastName);
    await this.companyInput.fill(user.company);
    await this.nextButton.click();
  }

  async fillStep3(user: { role: string; timezone: string }) {
    await this.roleSelect.selectOption(user.role);
    await this.timezoneSelect.selectOption(user.timezone);
    await this.submitButton.click();
  }

  async completeOnboarding(user: {
    email: string;
    password: string;
    firstName: string;
    lastName: string;
    company: string;
    role: string;
    timezone: string;
  }) {
    await this.fillStep1(user);
    await this.fillStep2(user);
    await this.fillStep3(user);
  }
}
```

## 5. Testes E2E Principais (`/tests/e2e/onboarding/onboarding.spec.ts`)

```typescript
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { OnboardingPage } from '../pages/OnboardingPage';
import { DashboardPage } from '../pages/DashboardPage';
import { TaskPage } from '../pages/TaskPage';
import { generateTestUser, generateTestTask } from '../fixtures/users';

test.describe('Onboarding Flow', () => {
  let onboardingPage: OnboardingPage;
  let dashboardPage: DashboardPage;
  let taskPage: TaskPage;
  const testUser = generateTestUser();
  const testTask = generateTestTask();

  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    dashboardPage = new DashboardPage(page);
    taskPage = new TaskPage(page);
    await onboardingPage.navigate();
  });

  test('should complete onboarding and create first task successfully', async ({ page }) => {
    // Step 1: Account creation
    await onboardingPage.fillStep1({
      email: testUser.email,
      password: testUser.password
    });
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/onboarding/step-2');

    // Step 2: Personal information
    await onboardingPage.fillStep2({
      firstName: testUser.firstName,
      lastName: testUser.lastName,
      company: testUser.company
    });
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/onboarding/step-3');

    // Step 3: Preferences
    await onboardingPage.fillStep3({
      role: testUser.role,
      timezone: testUser.timezone
    });

    // Verify dashboard is loaded
    await expect(dashboardPage.welcomeMessage).toHaveText(
      `Welcome, ${testUser.firstName}!`
    );
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/dashboard');

    // Create first task
    await dashboardPage.createTaskButton.click();
    await taskPage.fillTaskForm(testTask);
    await taskPage.submitButton.click();

    // Verify task was created
    await expect(taskPage.taskTitle).toHaveText(testTask.title);
    await expect(taskPage.taskDescription).toHaveText(testTask.description);
  });

  test('should show validation errors for empty required fields', async ({ page }) => {
    // Try to submit empty form
    await onboardingPage.nextButton.click();
    await expect(onboardingPage.errorMessage).toHaveText(
      'Email is required'
    );

    // Fill only email
    await onboardingPage.emailInput.fill(testUser.email);
    await onboardingPage.nextButton.click();
    await expect(onboardingPage.errorMessage).toHaveText(
      'Password is required'
    );
  });

  test('should recover from network error during onboarding', async ({ page }) => {
    // Mock network error
    await page.route('**/api/onboarding/step1', route => route.abort());

    await onboardingPage.fillStep1({
      email: testUser.email,
      password: testUser.password
    });

    await expect(onboardingPage.errorMessage).toHaveText(
      'Network error occurred. Please check your connection.'
    );

    // Retry with successful request
    await page.route('**/api/onboarding/step1', route =>
      route.fulfill({
        status: 200,
        contentType: 'application/json',
        body: JSON.stringify({ success: true })
      })
    );

    await onboardingPage.nextButton.click();
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/onboarding/step-2');
  });

  test('should persist onboarding progress when page is refreshed', async ({ page }) => {
    await onboardingPage.fillStep1({
      email: testUser.email,
      password: testUser.password
    });

    // Refresh page
    await page.reload();

    // Verify data is still there
    await expect(onboardingPage.emailInput).toHaveValue(testUser.email);
    await expect(onboardingPage.passwordInput).toHaveValue(testUser.password);
  });
});
```

## 6. Testes de Performance (`/tests/e2e/onboarding/performance.spec.ts`)

```typescript
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { OnboardingPage } from '../pages/OnboardingPage';
import { generateTestUser } from '../fixtures/users';

test.describe('Onboarding Performance', () => {
  test('should meet Core Web Vitals thresholds', async ({ page, browserName }) => {
    const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    const testUser = generateTestUser();

    // Enable performance metrics collection
    await page.goto('/onboarding', {
      waitUntil: 'networkidle'
    });

    // Measure Largest Contentful Paint (LCP)
    const lcpPromise = page.evaluate(() => {
      return new Promise<number>((resolve) => {
        new PerformanceObserver((entryList) => {
          const entries = entryList.getEntries();
          const lastEntry = entries[entries.length - 1];
          resolve(lastEntry.startTime);
        }).observe({
          type: 'largest-contentful-paint',
          buffered: true
        });
      });
    });

    // Complete onboarding
    await onboardingPage.completeOnboarding(testUser);

    // Get performance metrics
    const lcp = await lcpPromise;
    const metrics = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const [fid] = performance.getEntriesByName('first-input', 'measure');
      return {
        lcp: performance.getEntriesByType('largest-contentful-paint')[0]?.startTime,
        fid: fid?.duration || 0,
        cls: performance.getEntriesByType('layout-shift')[0]?.value || 0
      };
    });

    // Assert performance thresholds
    expect(metrics.lcp).toBeLessThan(2500); // LCP < 2.5s
    expect(metrics.fid).toBeLessThan(100); // FID < 100ms

    // Log metrics for reporting
    console.log(`Performance Metrics (${browserName}):`, {
      LCP: `${metrics.lcp.toFixed(2)}ms`,
      FID: `${metrics.fid.toFixed(2)}ms`,
      CLS: metrics.cls.toFixed(3)
    });
  });

  test('should maintain performance with multiple concurrent users', async ({ browser }) => {
    // This test would be run in CI with multiple workers
    // We'll simulate it by running the same test multiple times
    const testUser = generateTestUser();
    const contexts = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
      const context = await browser.newContext();
      const page = await context.newPage();
      const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);

      await onboardingPage.navigate();
      await onboardingPage.completeOnboarding({
        ...testUser,
        email: `user${i}@test.com`
      });

      contexts.push(context);
    }

    // Verify all sessions completed successfully
    for (const context of contexts) {
      const pages = context.pages();
      await expect(pages[0]).toHaveURL('/dashboard');
      await context.close();
    }
  });
});
```

## 7. Testes de Acessibilidade (`/tests/e2e/onboarding/accessibility.spec.ts`)

```typescript
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { OnboardingPage } from '../pages/OnboardingPage';
import AxeBuilder from '@axe-core/playwright';

test.describe('Onboarding Accessibility', () => {
  test('should have no accessibility violations', async ({ page }) => {
    const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    await onboardingPage.navigate();

    // Run axe accessibility checks
    const accessibilityScanResults = await new AxeBuilder({ page })
      .withTags(['wcag2a', 'wcag2aa', 'wcag21a', 'wcag21aa'])
      .analyze();

    // Log violations if any
    if (accessibilityScanResults.violations.length > 0) {
      console.log('Accessibility violations found:', accessibilityScanResults.violations);
    }

    // Assert no critical violations
    expect(accessibilityScanResults.violations).toEqual([]);
  });

  test('should be navigable with keyboard only', async ({ page }) => {
    const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    await onboardingPage.navigate();

    // Tab through the form
    await page.keyboard.press('Tab');
    await expect(onboardingPage.emailInput).toBeFocused();

    await page.keyboard.press('Tab');
    await expect(onboardingPage.passwordInput).toBeFocused();

    await page.keyboard.press('Tab');
    await expect(onboardingPage.nextButton).toBeFocused();

    // Fill form with keyboard
    await page.keyboard.type('test@example.com');
    await page.keyboard.press('Tab');
    await page.keyboard.type('password123');
    await page.keyboard.press('Enter');

    // Verify next step is reached
    await expect(page).toHaveURL('/onboarding/step-2');
  });

  test('should have proper ARIA attributes', async ({ page }) => {
    const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    await onboardingPage.navigate();

    // Check required fields have proper ARIA attributes
    await expect(onboardingPage.emailInput).toHaveAttribute('aria-required', 'true');
    await expect(onboardingPage.passwordInput).toHaveAttribute('aria-required', 'true');

    // Check error messages are properly associated
    await onboardingPage.nextButton.click();
    await expect(onboardingPage.errorMessage).toHaveAttribute(
      'aria-live',
      'assertive'
    );
  });
});
```

## 8. Smoke Tests para Pipeline de CI (`/tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts`)

```typescript
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { OnboardingPage } from './pages/OnboardingPage';
import { DashboardPage } from './pages/DashboardPage';
import { generateTestUser } from './fixtures/users';

test.describe('Smoke Tests', () => {
  test('critical onboarding flow should work in production', async ({ page }) => {
    const onboardingPage = new OnboardingPage(page);
    const dashboardPage = new DashboardPage(page);
    const testUser = generateTestUser();

    // This test would run against production after deploy
    await onboardingPage.navigate();

    // Verify basic page structure
    await expect(onboardingPage.emailInput).toBeVisible();
    await expect(onboardingPage.passwordInput).toBeVisible();
    await expect(onboardingPage.nextButton).toBeVisible();

    // Complete onboarding with minimal data
    await onboardingPage.completeOnboarding({
      ...testUser,
      firstName: 'Smoke',
      lastName: 'Test'
    });

    // Verify dashboard loads
    await expect(dashboardPage.welcomeMessage).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('should load main pages without errors', async ({ page }) => {
    const pagesToTest = [
      { url: '/', name: 'Homepage' },
      { url: '/onboarding', name: 'Onboarding' },
      { url: '/login', name: 'Login' },
      { url: '/dashboard', name: 'Dashboard' }
    ];

    for (const pageToTest of pagesToTest) {
      await test.step(`Testing ${pageToTest.name}`, async () => {
        const response = await page.goto(pageToTest.url);
        expect(response?.status()).toBeLessThan(400);
        await expect(page).toHaveTitle(/DIYAPP/);
      });
    }
  });
});
```

## 9. Integração com CI/CD

Adicione ao seu `package.json`:

```json
{
  "scripts": {
    "test:e2e": "playwright test tests/e2e/onboarding",
    "test:e2e:smoke": "playwright test tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts",
    "test:e2e:performance": "playwright test tests/e2e/onboarding/performance.spec.ts",
    "test:e2e:report": "playwright show-report test-results",
    "test:e2e:ci": "npm run test:e2e && npm run test:e2e:smoke"
  }
}
```

## 10. Critérios de Aceite para o Fluxo de Onboarding

```gherkin
Feature: User Onboarding
  As a new user
  I want to complete the onboarding process
  So that I can start using DIYAPP

  Scenario: Successful onboarding completion
    Given I am a new user on the onboarding page
    When I enter valid account information (email and password)
    And I enter my personal information (name, company)
    And I select my role and timezone
    And I submit the onboarding form
    Then I should be redirected to the dashboard
    And I should see a welcome message with my name
    And I should be able to create my first task

  Scenario: Validation errors for required fields
    Given I am on the onboarding page
    When I try to submit the form without filling required fields
    Then I should see validation errors for each empty required field
    And I should not be able to proceed to the next step

  Scenario: Network error recovery
    Given I am on the onboarding page
    When I submit the form and a network error occurs
    Then I should see an error message about the network issue
    And I should be able to retry the submission
    And when the network is restored, I should be able to proceed

  Scenario: Onboarding progress persistence
    Given I have partially completed the onboarding process
    When I refresh the page
    Then my previously entered information should still be there
    And I should be able to continue from where I left off

  Scenario: Performance requirements
    Given I am on the onboarding page
    When I complete the onboarding process
    Then the Largest Contentful Paint should be less than 2.5 seconds
    And the First Input Delay should be less than 100 milliseconds
    And the Cumulative Layout Shift should be less than 0.1
```

## 11. Monitoramento de Regressões

Adicione ao seu pipeline de CI (exemplo para GitHub Actions):

```yaml
name: E2E Tests

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 0 * * *' # Run daily

jobs:
  test:
    timeout-minutes: 60
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: 18
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: npm ci
    - name: Install Playwright Browsers
      run: npx playwright install --with-deps
    - name: Run E2E tests
      run: npm run test:e2e:ci
    - name: Upload test results
      if: always()
      uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
      with:
        name: playwright-report
        path: test-results/
        retention-days: 30
    - name: Check performance thresholds
      if: always()
      run: |
        # Parse performance results and fail if thresholds are exceeded
        node -e "
          const results = require('./test-results/results.json');
          const performanceTests = results.suites.flatMap(suite =>
            suite.specs.flatMap(spec =>
              spec.tests.flatMap(test =>
                test.results.filter(result =>
                  result.title.includes('Performance') &&
                  result.status === 'failed'
                )
              )
            )
          );

          if (performanceTests.length > 0) {
            console.log('Performance thresholds exceeded in tests:', performanceTests);
            process.exit(1);
          }
        "
```

Este plano de teste E2E abrangente cobre:
1. O fluxo crítico completo de onboarding
2. Validação de performance com métricas Core Web Vitals
3. Testes de acessibilidade
4. Recuperação de erros
5. Persistência de estado
6. Integração com CI/CD
7. Dados sintéticos para testes consistentes
8. Smoke tests para validação pós-deploy

A implementação segue a pirâmide de testes da squad com foco nos 10% de testes E2E que cobrem os fluxos críticos do usuário.

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core: Observability Stack

Vou instrumentar a aplicação com Prometheus para métricas, Jaeger para traces distribuídos, configurar alertas básicos e criar um dashboard no Grafana. Esta implementação seguirá as melhores práticas de observabilidade para aplicações modernas.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
/observability
  ├── prometheus/
  │   ├── prometheus.yml
  │   └── alert.rules
  ├── grafana/
  │   └── dashboards/
  │       └── diyapp-health-check.json
  ├── docker-compose.yml
  └── instrumentation/
      ├── metrics.js
      ├── tracing.js
      └── alerts.js
```

## 1. Configuração do Docker Compose (docker-compose.yml)

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Aplicação principal (DIYAPP)
  diyapp:
    image: diyapp:v12
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - JAEGER_AGENT_HOST=jaeger
      - JAEGER_AGENT_PORT=6831
      - PROMETHEUS_METRICS_PORT=9091
    depends_on:
      - jaeger
      - prometheus

  # Jaeger para traces distribuídos
  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:1.42
    ports:
      - "16686:16686" # UI
      - "6831:6831/udp" # Agent
      - "14268:14268" # HTTP collector
    environment:
      - COLLECTOR_ZIPKIN_HOST_PORT=:9411

  # Prometheus para métricas
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:v2.43.0
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - ./prometheus/alert.rules:/etc/prometheus/alert.rules
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'

  # Grafana para visualização
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:9.4.7
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./grafana/dashboards:/var/lib/grafana/dashboards
      - ./grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin
      - GF_USERS_ALLOW_SIGN_UP=false
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
```

## 2. Configuração do Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus.yml)

```yaml
global:
  scrape_interval: 15s
  evaluation_interval: 15s

rule_files:
  - 'alert.rules'

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'diyapp'
    metrics_path: '/metrics'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['diyapp:9091']

  - job_name: 'prometheus'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['localhost:9090']

alerting:
  alertmanagers:
    - static_configs:
        - targets:
          # Adicione seu Alertmanager aqui se necessário
```

## 3. Regras de Alertas (prometheus/alert.rules)

```yaml
groups:
- name: diyapp-alerts
  rules:
  - alert: HighLatencyP95
    expr: histogram_quantile(0.95, sum(rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) by (le, service)) > 1
    for: 5m
    labels:
      severity: critical
    annotations:
      summary: "High P95 latency detected (instance {{ $labels.instance }})"
      description: "P95 latency for service {{ $labels.service }} is {{ $value }}s (threshold: 1s)"

  - alert: HighErrorRate
    expr: rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5.."}[5m]) / rate(http_requests_total[5m]) > 0.01
    for: 5m
    labels:
      severity: critical
    annotations:
      summary: "High error rate detected (instance {{ $labels.instance }})"
      description: "Error rate for service {{ $labels.service }} is {{ $value }} (threshold: 1%)"

  - alert: ServiceDown
    expr: up{job="diyapp"} == 0
    for: 1m
    labels:
      severity: critical
    annotations:
      summary: "Service {{ $labels.job }} is down"
      description: "{{ $labels.job }} has been down for more than 1 minute"
```

## 4. Instrumentação da Aplicação (instrumentation/)

### metrics.js

```javascript
const promClient = require('prom-client');
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();

// Coleta métricas padrão
const collectDefaultMetrics = promClient.collectDefaultMetrics;
collectDefaultMetrics({ timeout: 5000 });

// Métricas customizadas
const httpRequestDurationMicroseconds = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code', 'service'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 0.7, 1, 3, 5, 7, 10] // buckets para latência
});

const httpRequestsTotal = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'http_requests_total',
  help: 'Total number of HTTP requests',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code', 'service']
});

const llmCallsTotal = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'llm_calls_total',
  help: 'Total number of LLM calls',
  labelNames: ['model', 'feature', 'status']
});

const llmCostTotal = new promClient.Gauge({
  name: 'llm_cost_total',
  help: 'Total cost of LLM calls in USD',
  labelNames: ['model', 'feature']
});

const llmLatencySeconds = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'llm_latency_seconds',
  help: 'Latency of LLM calls in seconds',
  labelNames: ['model', 'feature'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5, 10, 30] // buckets para latência de LLM
});

// Middleware para coletar métricas HTTP
function metricsMiddleware(req, res, next) {
  const end = httpRequestDurationMicroseconds.startTimer();
  const route = req.route?.path || req.path;

  res.on('finish', () => {
    const labels = {
      method: req.method,
      route: route,
      status_code: res.statusCode,
      service: 'diyapp'
    };

    httpRequestDurationMicroseconds.observe(labels, end());
    httpRequestsTotal.inc(labels);
  });

  next();
}

// Rota para expor métricas
router.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
  res.set('Content-Type', promClient.register.contentType);
  const metrics = await promClient.register.metrics();
  res.end(metrics);
});

// Funções para métricas de LLM
function trackLLMCall(model, feature, status, cost, latency) {
  llmCallsTotal.inc({ model, feature, status });
  llmCostTotal.inc({ model, feature }, cost);
  llmLatencySeconds.observe({ model, feature }, latency);
}

module.exports = {
  metricsMiddleware,
  trackLLMCall,
  router
};
```

### tracing.js

```javascript
const { initTracer } = require('jaeger-client');
const opentracing = require('opentracing');

// Configuração do Jaeger
function createTracer(serviceName) {
  const config = {
    serviceName: serviceName,
    sampler: {
      type: 'const',
      param: 1
    },
    reporter: {
      logSpans: true,
      agentHost: process.env.JAEGER_AGENT_HOST || 'localhost',
      agentPort: process.env.JAEGER_AGENT_PORT || 6831
    }
  };

  const options = {
    logger: {
      info(msg) { console.log(msg); },
      error(msg) { console.error(msg); }
    }
  };

  return initTracer(config, options);
}

// Middleware para tracing HTTP
function tracingMiddleware(req, res, next) {
  const tracer = req.app.get('tracer');
  const spanContext = tracer.extract(opentracing.FORMAT_HTTP_HEADERS, req.headers);
  const span = tracer.startSpan(req.path, { childOf: spanContext });

  span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.HTTP_METHOD, req.method);
  span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.SPAN_KIND, opentracing.Tags.SPAN_KIND_RPC_SERVER);
  span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.HTTP_URL, req.originalUrl);

  // Adiciona span ao request para uso posterior
  req.span = span;

  res.on('finish', () => {
    span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.HTTP_STATUS_CODE, res.statusCode);
    span.finish();
  });

  next();
}

// Função para tracing de chamadas LLM
function traceLLMCall(parentSpan, model, feature, operation) {
  const tracer = parentSpan.tracer();
  const span = tracer.startSpan(operation, { childOf: parentSpan });

  span.setTag('llm.model', model);
  span.setTag('llm.feature', feature);
  span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.SPAN_KIND, opentracing.Tags.SPAN_KIND_RPC_CLIENT);

  return {
    span,
    finish: (status, error) => {
      if (error) {
        span.setTag(opentracing.Tags.ERROR, true);
        span.log({ event: 'error', message: error.message });
      }
      span.setTag('llm.status', status);
      span.finish();
    }
  };
}

module.exports = {
  createTracer,
  tracingMiddleware,
  traceLLMCall
};
```

### alerts.js

```javascript
const promClient = require('prom-client');
const { createTracer } = require('./tracing');

// Métricas para alertas
const alertsTriggered = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'alerts_triggered_total',
  help: 'Total number of alerts triggered',
  labelNames: ['alertname', 'severity']
});

// Função para verificar alertas periodicamente
async function checkAlerts() {
  const tracer = createTracer('alert-manager');
  const span = tracer.startSpan('check_alerts');

  try {
    // Simulação de verificação de alertas (em produção, você faria queries reais)
    const highLatency = Math.random() > 0.9; // 10% de chance de alerta
    const highErrors = Math.random() > 0.95; // 5% de chance de alerta

    if (highLatency) {
      alertsTriggered.inc({ alertname: 'HighLatencyP95', severity: 'critical' });
      console.warn('ALERT: High P95 latency detected');
    }

    if (highErrors) {
      alertsTriggered.inc({ alertname: 'HighErrorRate', severity: 'critical' });
      console.warn('ALERT: High error rate detected');
    }

    span.log({ event: 'alert_check_completed' });
  } catch (error) {
    span.setTag('error', true);
    span.log({ event: 'error', message: error.message });
    console.error('Error checking alerts:', error);
  } finally {
    span.finish();
  }
}

// Configurar verificação periódica
setInterval(checkAlerts, 60000); // Verifica a cada minuto

module.exports = {
  alertsTriggered
};
```

```yaml
apiVersion: 1

datasources:
  - name: Prometheus
    type: prometheus
    access: proxy
    url: http://prometheus:9090
    isDefault: true
    editable: true
    jsonData:
      timeInterval: "5s"
```

apiVersion: 1

providers:

    orgId: 1
    folder: ''
    type: file
    disableDeletion: false
    updateIntervalSeconds: 10
    options:
      path: /var/lib/grafana/dashboards
```

## 8. Integração com a Aplicação Principal

Adicione ao seu `app.js` ou `server.js` principal:

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const { metricsMiddleware, router: metricsRouter } = require('./instrumentation/metrics');
const { createTracer, tracingMiddleware } = require('./instrumentation/tracing');
const { trackLLMCall } = require('./instrumentation/metrics');

const app = express();
const tracer = createTracer('diyapp');

// Middlewares de observabilidade
app.use(tracingMiddleware);
app.use(metricsMiddleware);

// Rotas
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.send('DIYAPP V12 - Observability Enabled');
});

// Rota para métricas
app.use('/metrics', metricsRouter);

// Exemplo de uso de LLM com observabilidade
app.post('/api/llm/:feature', async (req, res) => {
  const { feature } = req.params;
  const { prompt } = req.body;
  const model = 'gpt-4'; // ou qualquer modelo que você esteja usando

  // Inicia span para a chamada LLM
  const llmSpan = traceLLMCall(req.span, model, feature, 'llm_call');

  try {
    // Simulação de chamada LLM
    const startTime = Date.now();
    // ... sua lógica de chamada LLM aqui ...
    const response = await callLLM(model, prompt);
    const latency = (Date.now() - startTime) / 1000;
    const cost = calculateCost(model, prompt, response);

    // Registra métricas
    trackLLMCall(model, feature, 'success', cost, latency);

    llmSpan.finish('success');
    res.json(response);
  } catch (error) {
    // Registra métricas de erro
    trackLLMCall(model, feature, 'error', 0, 0);

    llmSpan.finish('error', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
});

async function callLLM(model, prompt) {
  // Implementação real da chamada ao LLM
  return { response: "Simulated LLM response" };
}

function calculateCost(model, prompt, response) {
  // Cálculo real do custo baseado em tokens
  return 0.01; // valor simulado
}

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`DIYAPP running on port ${PORT}`);
  console.log(`Metrics available at http://localhost:${PORT}/metrics`);
});
```

## Como Executar

1. Certifique-se de ter o Docker e Docker Compose instalados
2. Navegue até o diretório `/observability`
3. Execute:
   ```bash
   docker-compose up -d
   ```
4. Acesse os serviços:
   - Aplicação: http://localhost:3000
   - Grafana: http://localhost:3001 (usuário: admin, senha: admin)
   - Prometheus: http://localhost:9090
   - Jaeger: http://localhost:16686

## Funcionalidades Implementadas

1. **Métricas com Prometheus**:
   - Métricas HTTP padrão (latência, taxa de requisições, erros)
   - Métricas customizadas para LLM (custo, chamadas, latência)
   - Histogramas para análise de percentis

2. **Traces Distribuídos com Jaeger**:
   - Tracing de requisições HTTP
   - Tracing de chamadas LLM com contexto
   - Integração com middleware Express

3. **Alertas**:
   - Latência P95 > 1s
   - Taxa de erros > 1%
   - Serviço indisponível
   - Configuração no Prometheus com regras de alerta

4. **Dashboard no Grafana**:
   - Visão geral da aplicação
   - Métricas de requisições (taxa, erros, latência)
   - Métricas específicas de LLM
   - Lista de alertas ativos
   - Provisionamento automático de dashboards

5. **Integração com LLM Gateway**:
   - Métricas específicas para monitoramento de LLMs
   - Rastreamento de custo por modelo e feature
   - Latência de chamadas LLM

Esta implementação fornece uma base sólida para observabilidade da DIYAPP V12, permitindo monitoramento em tempo real, detecção de anomalias e análise de desempenho conforme as responsabilidades do AI Ops definidas no contexto.

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core: Eventos de Usuário Pipeline

Vou estruturar o projeto com foco em:
1. Schema de eventos (Avro/JSON Schema)
2. Pipeline de ingestão (Kafka + Vector)
3. Views materializadas para analytics
4. Modo Hive para refatoração paralela

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── /schemas
│   ├── user_events.avsc          # Schema Avro para eventos
│   └── user_events.json          # Schema JSON alternativo

## 1. Schema de Eventos (Avro/JSON Schema)

### `schemas/user_events.avsc` (Avro Schema)
```json
{
  "type": "record",
  "name": "UserEvent",
  "namespace": "com.diyapp.events",
  "doc": "Schema para eventos de usuário do DIYAPP Evolution V12",
  "fields": [
    {
      "name": "event_id",
      "type": "string",
      "doc": "UUID único do evento"
    },
    {
      "name": "user_id",
      "type": "string",
      "doc": "ID do usuário (anônimo ou autenticado)"
    },
    {
      "name": "session_id",
      "type": "string",
      "doc": "ID da sessão do usuário"
    },
    {
      "name": "event_type",
      "type": {
        "type": "enum",
        "name": "EventType",
        "symbols": [
          "PAGE_VIEW",
          "BUTTON_CLICK",
          "API_CALL",
          "ERROR",
          "PERFORMANCE",
          "FEATURE_USAGE",
          "AUTHENTICATION"
        ]
      },
      "doc": "Tipo do evento"
    },
    {
      "name": "event_timestamp",
      "type": "long",
      "logicalType": "timestamp-millis",
      "doc": "Timestamp do evento em milissegundos (UTC)"
    },
    {
      "name": "app_version",
      "type": "string",
      "doc": "Versão do aplicativo que gerou o evento"
    },
    {
      "name": "os",
      "type": ["null", "string"],
      "default": null,
      "doc": "Sistema operacional do dispositivo"
    },
    {
      "name": "device_type",
      "type": ["null", "string"],
      "default": null,
      "doc": "Tipo de dispositivo (mobile, desktop, tablet)"
    },
    {
      "name": "country",
      "type": ["null", "string"],
      "default": null,
      "doc": "País do usuário (ISO 3166-1 alpha-2)"
    },
    {
      "name": "metadata",
      "type": {
        "type": "map",
        "values": "string"
      },
      "doc": "Metadados específicos do evento (ex: page_url, button_id, etc)"
    },
    {
      "name": "performance_data",
      "type": [
        "null",
        {
          "type": "record",
          "name": "PerformanceData",
          "fields": [
            {"name": "load_time_ms", "type": "int"},
            {"name": "ttfb_ms", "type": "int"},
            {"name": "resource_size_kb", "type": "int"},
            {"name": "fps", "type": ["null", "int"], "default": null}
          ]
        }
      ],
      "default": null,
      "doc": "Dados de performance (apenas para eventos PERFORMANCE)"
    },
    {
      "name": "error_data",
      "type": [
        "null",
        {
          "type": "record",
          "name": "ErrorData",
          "fields": [
            {"name": "error_code", "type": "string"},
            {"name": "error_message", "type": "string"},
            {"name": "stack_trace", "type": ["null", "string"], "default": null},
            {"name": "severity", "type": "string"}
          ]
        }
      ],
      "default": null,
      "doc": "Dados de erro (apenas para eventos ERROR)"
    }
  ]
}
```

### `schemas/user_events.json` (JSON Schema alternativo)
```json
{
  "$schema": "http://json-schema.org/draft-07/schema#",

## 2. Pipeline de Ingestão (Kafka + Vector)

### `ingestion/docker-compose.yml`
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  zookeeper:
    image: confluentinc/cp-zookeeper:7.3.0
    environment:
      ZOOKEEPER_CLIENT_PORT: 2181
      ZOOKEEPER_TICK_TIME: 2000
    ports:
      - "2181:2181"

  kafka:
    image: confluentinc/cp-kafka:7.3.0
    depends_on:
      - zookeeper
    ports:
      - "9092:9092"
    environment:
      KAFKA_BROKER_ID: 1
      KAFKA_ZOOKEEPER_CONNECT: zookeeper:2181
      KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://kafka:9092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://localhost:29092
      KAFKA_LISTENER_SECURITY_PROTOCOL_MAP: PLAINTEXT:PLAINTEXT,PLAINTEXT_HOST:PLAINTEXT
      KAFKA_INTER_BROKER_LISTENER_NAME: PLAINTEXT
      KAFKA_OFFSETS_TOPIC_REPLICATION_FACTOR: 1
      KAFKA_AUTO_CREATE_TOPICS_ENABLE: "true"

  vector:
    image: timberio/vector:0.32.0-debian
    volumes:
      - ./vector-config:/etc/vector
    depends_on:
      - kafka
    ports:
      - "8686:8686" # API
      - "9000:9000" # HTTP source
    environment:
      VECTOR_LOG: "info"

  schema-registry:
    image: confluentinc/cp-schema-registry:7.3.0
    depends_on:
      - kafka
    ports:
      - "8081:8081"
    environment:
      SCHEMA_REGISTRY_HOST_NAME: schema-registry
      SCHEMA_REGISTRY_KAFKASTORE_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS: kafka:9092
      SCHEMA_REGISTRY_LISTENERS: http://0.0.0.0:8081
```

### `ingestion/kafka-config/producer-config.json`
```json
{
  "bootstrap.servers": "kafka:9092",
  "client.id": "diyapp-producer",
  "acks": "all",
  "retries": 3,
  "compression.type": "snappy",
  "key.serializer": "org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringSerializer",
  "value.serializer": "io.confluent.kafka.serializers.KafkaAvroSerializer",
  "schema.registry.url": "http://schema-registry:8081",
  "max.in.flight.requests.per.connection": 5,
  "enable.idempotence": true
}
```

### `ingestion/vector-config/vector.toml`
```toml
[data_dir]
path = "/var/lib/vector"

# API para monitoramento
[api]
enabled = true
address = "0.0.0.0:8686"

# Fonte HTTP para receber eventos
[sources.http_events]
type = "http_server"
address = "0.0.0.0:9000"
encoding.codec = "json"

# Transformação para validar e enriquecer eventos
[transforms.process_events]
type = "remap"
inputs = ["http_events"]
source = '''
# Adiciona timestamp de processamento se não existir
if !exists(.processing_timestamp) {
  .processing_timestamp = to_unix_timestamp(now())
}

# Validação básica do schema
if !exists(.event_id) || !exists(.user_id) || !exists(.event_type) {
  abort
}

# Normaliza campos
if exists(.event_timestamp) {
  .event_timestamp = to_unix_timestamp(parse_timestamp!(.event_timestamp, format: "%+"))
}
'''

# Roteamento para Kafka
[sinks.kafka_events]
type = "kafka"
inputs = ["process_events"]
bootstrap_servers = "kafka:9092"
topic = "diyapp-user-events"
key_field = "event_id"
compression = "snappy"
encoding.codec = "json"

# Configuração para modo Hive (backup em S3/HDFS)
[sinks.s3_backup]
type = "aws_s3"
inputs = ["process_events"]
bucket = "diyapp-events-backup"
key_prefix = "year=%Y/month=%m/day=%d/hour=%H/"
region = "us-east-1"
encoding.codec = "json"
compression = "gzip"
batch.max_bytes = 10485760 # 10MB
```

### `ingestion/vector-config/transforms.yaml`
```yaml
transforms:
  - type: remap
    inputs:
      - http_events
    source: |
      # Adiciona metadados de processamento
      .vector_ingested_at = now()
      .vector_source = "http"

      # Normaliza campos de performance
      if exists(.performance_data) {
        .performance_data.load_time_ms = to_int(.performance_data.load_time_ms) ?? 0
        .performance_data.ttfb_ms = to_int(.performance_data.ttfb_ms) ?? 0
        .performance_data.resource_size_kb = to_int(.performance_data.resource_size_kb) ?? 0
      }

      # Normaliza campos de erro
      if exists(.error_data) {
        .error_data.severity = upcase!(.error_data.severity)
      }

      # Garante que campos obrigatórios existem
      .event_id = .event_id ?? uuid_v4()
      .user_id = .user_id ?? "anonymous"
      .session_id = .session_id ?? uuid_v4()
      .event_type = upcase!(.event_type ?? "UNKNOWN")
      .event_timestamp = .event_timestamp ?? to_unix_timestamp(now())
      .app_version = .app_version ?? "unknown"
      .metadata = .metadata ?? {}
```

## 3. Views Materializadas para Analytics

### `analytics/dbt/dbt_project.yml`
```yaml
name: 'diyapp_analytics'

profile: 'diyapp'

test-paths: ["tests"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_analytics:
    staging:
      +materialized: view
      +schema: staging
    marts:
      +materialized: table
      +schema: analytics
      +tags: ["marts"]
    materialized_views:
      +materialized: incremental
      +schema: analytics
      +tags: ["materialized_views"]
      +incremental_strategy: merge
      +unique_key: id
```

### `analytics/dbt/models/schema.yml`
```yaml
version: 2

sources:
  - name: raw_events
    database: diyapp
    schema: raw
    tables:
      - name: user_events
        description: "Eventos brutos de usuários coletados via Kafka"
        columns:
          - name: event_id
            description: "UUID único do evento"
            tests:
              - not_null
              - unique
          - name: user_id
            description: "ID do usuário"
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: event_type
            description: "Tipo do evento"
            tests:
              - not_null
              - accepted_values:
                  values: ['PAGE_VIEW', 'BUTTON_CLICK', 'API_CALL', 'ERROR', 'PERFORMANCE', 'FEATURE_USAGE', 'AUTHENTICATION']
          - name: event_timestamp
            description: "Timestamp do evento"
            tests:
              - not_null
          - name: app_version
            description: "Versão do aplicativo"
            tests:
              - not_null

models:
  - name: stg_user_events
    description: "Eventos de usuário limpos e padronizados"
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        tests:
          - not_null
          - unique
      - name: user_id
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: session_id
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: event_type
        tests:
          - not_null

              values: ['PAGE_VIEW', 'BUTTON_CLICK', 'API_CALL', 'ERROR', 'PERFORMANCE', 'FEATURE_USAGE', 'AUTHENTICATION']
      - name: event_timestamp
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: app_version
        tests:
          - not_null

          - accepted_values:
              values: ['iOS', 'Android', 'Windows', 'macOS', 'Linux', null]

              quote: false

  - name: mart_user_engagement
